<pr_description>
Intermittent failures with ServerResponse.outputStream() and static file serving
## Environment Details

## Problem Description
I've seen two maybe related problems while using outputStream(). The same issues seem to affect `helidon-webserver-static-content`. See Steps to reproduce below for details.

If using chunked transfer, I occasionally see "missing CR"  or "Malformed encoding found in chunked-encoding" or something similar depending on client.

If sending content-length header, the transfer occasionally just gets stuck completely. `StaticContentFeature` does this, so it is also affected.

100MB files trigger the problems more often, but I've managed to reproduce them also with 10MB files.

These have been tested with multiple client (`curl`, `java.net.http.HttpClient` and `HttpURLConnection`).

On server side I get the following trace:

## Steps to reproduce

Here's a sample program that provides 
* `/fixed` -> content length header, gets stuck
* `/chunked` -> CR failure
* `/dynamic` -> CR failure, no file system used to rule that out
* `/static` -> same as `/fixed` but through `StaticContentFeature`

```java
import io.helidon.http.HeaderNames;
import io.helidon.webserver.WebServer;
import io.helidon.webserver.staticcontent.StaticContentFeature;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.io.OutputStream;
import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;

public class Main {

    static void main() throws Exception {
        var path = Files.createTempFile("helidon-output-test", null);
        path.toFile().deleteOnExit();

        var size = 100_000_000;
        fillTestFile(path, size);

        WebServer.builder()
            .port(8080)
            .routing(routing -> {
                routing.any("/fixed", (_, res) -> {
                    res.status(200);
                    res.header(HeaderNames.CONTENT_TYPE_NAME, "octet-stream");
                    res.contentLength(size);
                    try (var out = res.outputStream(); var in = Files.newInputStream(path)) {
                        in.transferTo(out);
                    }
                });
                routing.any("/chunked", (_, res) -> {
                    res.status(200);
                    res.header(HeaderNames.CONTENT_TYPE_NAME, "octet-stream");
                    try (var out = res.outputStream(); var in = Files.newInputStream(path)) {
                        in.transferTo(out);
                    }
                });
                routing.any("/dynamic", (_, res) -> {
                    res.status(200);
                    res.header(HeaderNames.CONTENT_TYPE_NAME, "octet-stream");
                    try (var out = res.outputStream()) {
                        fillOutput(out, size);
                    }
                });
            })
            .addFeature(StaticContentFeature.builder()
                .addPath(p -> p.location(path).context("/static"))
                .build())
            .build()
            .start();
    }

    private static void fillOutput(OutputStream out, long size) throws IOException {
        var source = "xy".repeat(524_288).getBytes();

        var remaining = size;
        while (remaining > 0) {
            var chunk = (int) Math.min(source.length, remaining);
            out.write(source, 0, chunk);
            remaining -= chunk;
        }
    }

    private static void fillTestFile(Path path, long size) throws IOException {
        try (var os = Files.newOutputStream(path)) {
            fillOutput(os, size);
        }
    }

}

```

Malformed chunked body after upgrading from 4.3.4 to 4.4.0
## Environment Details
* Helidon Version: 4.4.0
* Helidon MP
* JDK version: 25.0.2
* OS: Alpaquita Linux Container

----------

## Problem Description

After upgrading our service from Helidon **4.3.4** to **4.4.0**, we started seeing rare, nondeterministic failures in service-to-service integrations.

The failures happen only occasionally and are difficult to reproduce locally, but they can be triggered during load testing in the deployed environment.

The client receives errors indicating that the HTTP/1.1 chunked response is malformed, for example:

    24	import java.util.List;
    25	import java.util.Objects;
    26	import java.util.ServiceLoader;
    27	import java.util.function.Consumer;
    28	import java.util.function.Supplier;
    29	import java.util.function.UnaryOperator;

    32	import io.helidon.common.HelidonServiceLoader;

    34	import io.helidon.common.buffers.DataWriter;
    35	import io.helidon.common.media.type.MediaType;
    36	import io.helidon.common.media.type.MediaTypes;

    39	import io.helidon.http.HeaderNames;
    40	import io.helidon.http.HeaderValues;
    41	import io.helidon.http.HttpException;
    42	import io.helidon.http.ServerResponseHeaders;

    48	import io.helidon.webserver.ConnectionContext;

    56	
    57	/**
    58	 * An HTTP/1 server response.
    59	 */
    60	class Http1ServerResponse extends ServerResponseBase<Http1ServerResponse> {
    61	    private static final System.Logger LOGGER = System.getLogger(Http1ServerResponse.class.getName());
    62	    private static final byte[] HTTP_BYTES = "HTTP/1.1 ".getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    63	    private static final byte[] OK_200 = "HTTP/1.1 200 OK\r\n".getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    64	    private static final byte[] DATE = "Date: ".getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    65	    private static final byte[] TERMINATING_CHUNK = "0\r\n\r\n".getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    66	    private static final byte[] TERMINATING_CHUNK_TRAILERS = "0\r\n".getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    67	
    68	    @SuppressWarnings("rawtypes")
    69	    private static final List<SinkProvider> SINK_PROVIDERS
    70	            = HelidonServiceLoader.builder(ServiceLoader.load(SinkProvider.class)).build().asList();
    71	    private static final WritableHeaders<?> EMPTY_HEADERS = WritableHeaders.create();
    72	
    73	    private final ConnectionContext ctx;
    74	    private final Http1ConnectionListener sendListener;
    75	    private final DataWriter dataWriter;
    76	    private final Http1ServerRequest request;
    77	    private final ServerResponseHeaders headers;
    78	    private final ServerResponseTrailers trailers;
    79	    private final boolean keepAlive;
    80	
    81	    private boolean streamingEntity;
    82	    private boolean isSent;
    83	    private ClosingBufferedOutputStream outputStream;
    84	    private long bytesWritten;
    85	    private String streamResult = "";
    86	    private boolean isNoEntityStatus;
    87	    private final boolean validateHeaders;
    88	
    89	    private UnaryOperator<OutputStream> outputStreamFilter;
    90	
    91	    Http1ServerResponse(ConnectionContext ctx,
    92	                        Http1ConnectionListener sendListener,
    93	                        DataWriter dataWriter,
    94	                        Http1ServerRequest request,
    95	                        boolean keepAlive,
    96	                        boolean validateHeaders) {
    97	        super(ctx, request);
    98	
    99	        this.ctx = ctx;
   100	        this.sendListener = sendListener;
   101	        this.dataWriter = dataWriter;
   102	        this.request = request;
   103	        this.headers = ServerResponseHeaders.create();
   104	        this.trailers = ServerResponseTrailers.create();
   105	        this.keepAlive = keepAlive;
   106	        this.validateHeaders = validateHeaders;
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    static void nonEntityBytes(ServerResponseHeaders headers,
   110	                               Status status,
   111	                               BufferData buffer,
   112	                               boolean keepAlive,
   113	                               boolean validateHeaders) {
   114	
   115	        status = status == null ? Status.OK_200 : status;
   116	
   117	        if (isNoEntityStatus(status)) {
   118	            // https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9110#status.204
   119	            // A 204 response is terminated by the end of the header section; it cannot contain content or trailers
   120	            // ditto for 205, and 304
   121	            if ((headers.contains(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH) && !headers.contains(HeaderValues.CONTENT_LENGTH_ZERO))
   122	                         || headers.contains(HeaderValues.TRANSFER_ENCODING_CHUNKED)) {
   123	                status = noEntityInternalError(status);
   124	            }
   125	        }
   126	
   127	        // first write status
   128	        if (status == Status.OK_200) {
   129	            buffer.write(OK_200);
   130	        } else {
   131	            buffer.write(HTTP_BYTES);
   132	            String reasonPhrase = status.reasonPhrase() == null || status.reasonPhrase().isEmpty()
   133	                    ? status.codeText() : status.reasonPhrase();
   134	            buffer.write((status.code() + " " + reasonPhrase).getBytes(StandardCharsets.US_ASCII));
   135	            buffer.write('\r');
   136	            buffer.write('\n');
   137	        }
   138	        // date header
   139	        if (!headers.contains(HeaderNames.DATE)) {
   140	            buffer.write(DATE);
   141	            byte[] dateBytes = DateTime.http1Bytes();
   142	            buffer.write(dateBytes);
   143	        }
   144	
   145	        // either content-length or chunked encoding
   146	        // if content length - make sure to compare it when writing actual entity (streaming and send(entity))
   147	        if (keepAlive) {
   148	            headers.setIfAbsent(HeaderValues.CONNECTION_KEEP_ALIVE);
   149	        } else {
   150	            // we must override even if user sets keep alive, as close was requested
   151	            headers.set(HeaderValues.CONNECTION_CLOSE);
   152	        }
   153	
   154	        // write headers followed by empty line
   155	        writeHeaders(headers, buffer, validateHeaders);
   156	
   157	        buffer.write('\r');        // "\r\n" - empty line after headers
   158	        buffer.write('\n');
   159	    }
   160	
   161	    @Override
   162	    public Http1ServerResponse status(Status status) {
   163	        // set internal state
   164	        super.status(status);
   165	        isNoEntityStatus = isNoEntityStatus(status);
   166	
   167	        // check consistency if status code should not include entity
   168	        if (isNoEntityStatus) {
   169	            if (!headers.contains(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH)) {
   170	                headers.set(HeaderValues.CONTENT_LENGTH_ZERO);
   171	            } else if (headers.get(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH).getLong() > 0L) {
   172	                throw new IllegalStateException("Cannot set status to " + status + " with header "
   173	                                                        + HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH + " greater than zero");
   174	            }
   175	        }
   176	        return this;
   177	    }
   178	
   179	    @Override
   180	    public Http1ServerResponse header(Header header) {
   181	        if (streamingEntity) {
   182	            throw new IllegalStateException("Cannot set response header after requesting output stream.");
   183	        }
   184	        if (isSent()) {
   185	            throw new IllegalStateException("Cannot set response header after response was already sent.");
   186	        }
   187	        this.headers.set(header);
   188	        return this;
   189	    }
   190	
   191	    /**
   192	     * Actually send the response over the wire, if allowed by status code.
   193	     */
   194	    @Override
   195	    public void send(byte[] bytes) {
   196	        send(bytes, 0, bytes.length);
   197	    }
   198	
   199	    @Override
   200	    public void send(byte[] bytes, int position, int length) {
   201	        // if no entity status, we cannot send bytes here
   202	        if (isNoEntityStatus && length > 0) {
   203	            status(noEntityInternalError(status()));
   204	            return;
   205	        }
   206	
   207	        // send bytes to writer
   208	        beforeSend();
   209	
   210	        if (outputStreamFilter == null && !headers.contains(HeaderNames.TRAILER)) {
   211	            byte[] entity = entityBytes(bytes, position, length);
   212	            BufferData bufferData = (bytes != entity) ? responseBuffer(entity)
   213	                    : responseBuffer(entity, position, length);         // no encoding, same length
   214	            bytesWritten = bufferData.available();
   215	            isSent = true;
   216	            request.reset();
   217	            dataWriter.write(bufferData);
   218	            afterSend();
   219	        } else {
   220	            // we should skip encoders if no data is written (e.g. for GZIP)
   221	            boolean skipEncoders = (length == 0);
   222	            try (OutputStream os = outputStream(skipEncoders)) {
   223	                os.write(bytes, position, length);
   224	            } catch (IOException e) {
   225	                throw new ServerConnectionException("Failed to write response", e);
   226	            }
   227	            // after send is part of the output stream handling
   228	        }
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    @Override
   232	    public boolean isSent() {
   233	        return isSent;
   234	    }
   235	
   236	    @Override
   237	    public OutputStream outputStream() {
   238	        beforeSend();
   239	        return outputStream(false);
   240	    }
   241	
   242	    @Override
   243	    public long bytesWritten() {
   244	        if (streamingEntity) {
   245	            return outputStream.totalBytesWritten();
   246	        } else {
   247	            return bytesWritten;
   248	        }
   249	    }
   250	
   251	    @Override
   252	    public ServerResponseHeaders headers() {
   253	        return headers;
   254	    }
   255	
   256	    @Override
   257	    public ServerResponseTrailers trailers() {
   258	        if (request.headers().contains(HeaderValues.TE_TRAILERS) || headers.contains(HeaderNames.TRAILER)) {
   259	            return trailers;
   260	        }
   261	        throw new IllegalStateException(
   262	                "Trailers are supported only when request came with 'TE: trailers' header or "
   263	                        + "response headers have trailer names definition 'Trailer: <trailer-name>'");
   264	    }
   265	
   266	    @Override
   267	    public void streamResult(String result) {
   268	        this.streamResult = result;
   269	        if (outputStream != null) {
   270	            outputStream.close();
   271	        }
   272	    }
   273	
   274	    @Override
   275	    public boolean hasEntity() {
   276	        return isSent || streamingEntity;
   277	    }
   278	
   279	    @Override
   280	    public boolean reset() {
   281	        if (isSent || outputStream != null && outputStream.totalBytesWritten() > 0) {
   282	            return false;
   283	        }
   284	        headers.clear();
   285	        streamingEntity = false;
   286	        outputStream = null;
   287	        return true;
   288	    }
   289	
   290	    @Override
   291	    public boolean resetStream() {
   292	        if (isSent || outputStream != null && outputStream.totalBytesWritten() > 0) {
   293	            return false;
   294	        }
   295	        streamingEntity = false;
   296	        outputStream = null;
   297	        return true;
   298	    }
   299	
   300	    @Override
   301	    public void commit() {
   302	        if (outputStream != null) {
   303	            outputStream.commit();
   304	        }
   305	    }
   306	
   307	    @Override
   308	    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   309	    public <X extends Sink<?>> X sink(GenericType<X> sinkType) {
   310	        for (SinkProvider<?> p : SINK_PROVIDERS) {
   311	            if (p.supports(sinkType, request)) {
   312	                try {
   313	                    return (X) p.create(new SinkProviderContext() {
   314	                        @Override
   315	                        public ServerResponse serverResponse() {
   316	                            return Http1ServerResponse.this;
   317	                        }
   318	
   319	                        @Override
   320	                        public ServerRequest serverRequest() {
   321	                            return Http1ServerResponse.this.request;
   322	                        }
   323	
   324	                        @Override
   325	                        public ConnectionContext connectionContext() {
   326	                            return Http1ServerResponse.this.ctx;
   327	                        }
   328	
   329	                        @Override
   330	                        public Runnable closeRunnable() {
   331	                            return () -> {
   332	                                Http1ServerResponse.this.isSent = true;
   333	                                afterSend();
   334	                                request.reset();
   335	                            };
   336	                        }
   337	                    });
   338	                } catch (UnsupportedOperationException e) {
   339	                    // deprecated - will be removed in 5.x
   340	                    return (X) p.create(this, this::handleSinkData, this::commit);
   341	                }
   342	            }
   343	        }
   344	        // Request not acceptable if provider not found
   345	        throw new HttpException("Unable to find sink provider for request", Status.NOT_ACCEPTABLE_406);
   346	    }
   347	
   348	    @Override
   349	    public void streamFilter(UnaryOperator<OutputStream> filterFunction) {
   350	        if (isSent) {
   351	            throw new IllegalStateException("Response already sent");
   352	        }
   353	        if (streamingEntity) {
   354	            throw new IllegalStateException("OutputStream already obtained");
   355	        }
   356	        Objects.requireNonNull(filterFunction);
   357	        UnaryOperator<OutputStream> current = this.outputStreamFilter;
   358	        if (current == null) {
   359	            this.outputStreamFilter = filterFunction;
   360	        } else {
   361	            this.outputStreamFilter = it -> filterFunction.apply(current.apply(it));
   362	        }
   363	    }
   364	
   365	    private void handleSinkData(Object data, MediaType mediaType) {
   366	        if (outputStream == null) {
   367	            outputStream();
   368	        }
   369	        try {
   370	            MediaContext mediaContext = mediaContext();
   371	
   372	            if (data instanceof byte[] bytes) {
   373	                outputStream.write(bytes);
   374	            } else {
   375	                if (data instanceof String str && mediaType.equals(MediaTypes.TEXT_PLAIN)) {
   376	                    EntityWriter<String> writer = mediaContext.writer(GenericType.STRING, EMPTY_HEADERS, EMPTY_HEADERS);
   377	                    writer.write(GenericType.STRING, str, outputStream, EMPTY_HEADERS, EMPTY_HEADERS);
   378	                } else {
   379	                    GenericType<Object> type = GenericType.create(data);
   380	                    WritableHeaders<?> resHeaders = WritableHeaders.create();
   381	                    resHeaders.set(HeaderNames.CONTENT_TYPE, mediaType.text());
   382	                    EntityWriter<Object> writer = mediaContext.writer(type, EMPTY_HEADERS, resHeaders);
   383	                    writer.write(type, data, outputStream, EMPTY_HEADERS, resHeaders);
   384	                }
   385	            }
   386	        } catch (IOException e) {
   387	            throw new ServerConnectionException("Failed to write sink data", e);
   388	        }
   389	    }
   390	
   391	    private static void writeHeaders(io.helidon.http.Headers headers, BufferData buffer, boolean validate) {
   392	        if (validate) {
   393	            headers.forEach(Header::validate);
   394	        }
   395	        for (Header header : headers) {
   396	            header.writeHttp1Header(buffer);
   397	        }
   398	    }
   399	
   400	    private BufferData responseBuffer(byte[] bytes) {
   401	        return responseBuffer(bytes, 0, bytes.length);
   402	    }
   403	
   404	    private BufferData responseBuffer(byte[] bytes, int position, int length) {
   405	        if (isSent) {
   406	            throw new IllegalStateException("Response already sent");
   407	        }
   408	        if (streamingEntity) {
   409	            throw new IllegalStateException("When output stream is used, response is completed by closing the output stream"
   410	                                                    + ", do not call send().");
   411	        }
   412	
   413	        boolean forcedChunkedEncoding = false;
   414	        headers.setIfAbsent(HeaderValues.CONNECTION_KEEP_ALIVE);
   415	
   416	        if (headers.contains(HeaderNames.TRANSFER_ENCODING) && headers.contains(HeaderValues.TRANSFER_ENCODING_CHUNKED)) {
   417	            headers.remove(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH);
   418	            // chunked enforced (and even if empty entity, will be used)
   419	            forcedChunkedEncoding = true;
   420	        } else if (!headers.contains(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH)) {
   421	            headers.contentLength(length);
   422	        }
   423	
   424	        Status usedStatus = status();
   425	        sendListener.status(ctx, usedStatus);
   426	        sendListener.headers(ctx, headers);
   427	
   428	        // give some space for code and headers + entity
   429	        BufferData responseBuffer = BufferData.growing(256 + length);
   430	
   431	        nonEntityBytes(headers, usedStatus, responseBuffer, keepAlive, validateHeaders);
   432	        if (forcedChunkedEncoding) {
   433	            byte[] hex = Integer.toHexString(length).getBytes(StandardCharsets.US_ASCII);
   434	            responseBuffer.write(hex);
   435	            responseBuffer.write('\r');
   436	            responseBuffer.write('\n');
   437	            responseBuffer.write(bytes, position, length);
   438	            responseBuffer.write('\r');
   439	            responseBuffer.write('\n');
   440	            responseBuffer.write(TERMINATING_CHUNK);
   441	        } else {
   442	            responseBuffer.write(bytes, position, length);
   443	        }
   444	
   445	        sendListener.data(ctx, responseBuffer);
   446	
   447	        return responseBuffer;
   448	    }
   449	
   450	    private OutputStream outputStream(boolean skipEncoders) {
   451	        if (isSent) {
   452	            throw new IllegalStateException("Response already sent");
   453	        }
   454	        if (streamingEntity) {
   455	            throw new IllegalStateException("OutputStream already obtained");
   456	        }
   457	        streamingEntity = true;
   458	
   459	        BlockingOutputStream bos = new BlockingOutputStream(headers,
   460	                                                            trailers,
   461	                                                            beforeTrailers(),
   462	                                                            this::status,
   463	                                                            () -> streamResult,
   464	                                                            dataWriter,
   465	                                                            () -> {
   466	                                                                this.isSent = true;
   467	                                                                afterSend();
   468	                                                                request.reset();
   469	                                                            },
   470	                                                            ctx,
   471	                                                            sendListener,
   472	                                                            request,
   473	                                                            keepAlive,
   474	                                                            validateHeaders,
   475	                                                            isNoEntityStatus);
   476	
   477	        int writeBufferSize = ctx.listenerContext().config().writeBufferSize();
   478	        outputStream = new ClosingBufferedOutputStream(bos, writeBufferSize);
   479	
   480	        OutputStream encodedOutputStream = outputStream;
   481	        if (!skipEncoders) {
   482	            encodedOutputStream = contentEncode(outputStream);
   483	            bos.checkResponseHeaders();     // headers can be augmented by encoders
   484	        }
   485	        return outputStreamFilter == null ? encodedOutputStream : outputStreamFilter.apply(encodedOutputStream);
   486	    }
   487	
   488	    private static Status noEntityInternalError(Status status) {
   489	        LOGGER.log(System.Logger.Level.ERROR, "Attempt to send status " + status.text() + " with entity."
   490	                + " Server responded with Internal Server Error. Please fix your routing, this is not allowed "
   491	                + "by HTTP specification, such responses MUST NOT contain an entity.");
   492	        return Status.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR_500;
   493	    }
   494	
   495	    private static boolean isNoEntityStatus(Status status) {
   496	        int code = status.code();
   497	        return code == Status.NO_CONTENT_204.code()
   498	                || code == Status.RESET_CONTENT_205.code()
   499	                || code == Status.NOT_MODIFIED_304.code();
   500	    }
   501	
   502	    static class BlockingOutputStream extends OutputStream {
   503	        private final ServerResponseHeaders headers;
   504	        private final WritableHeaders<?> trailers;
   505	        private final Supplier<Status> status;
   506	        private final DataWriter dataWriter;
   507	        private final Runnable responseCloseRunnable;
   508	        private final ConnectionContext ctx;
   509	        private final Http1ConnectionListener sendListener;
   510	        private final Http1ServerRequest request;
   511	        private final boolean keepAlive;
   512	        private final Supplier<String> streamResult;
   513	        private boolean forcedChunked;
   514	
   515	        private BufferData firstBuffer;
   516	        private boolean closed;
   517	        private long bytesWritten;
   518	        private long contentLength;
   519	        private boolean isChunked;
   520	        private boolean firstByte = true;
   521	        private long responseBytesTotal;
   522	        private boolean closing = false;
   523	        private final boolean validateHeaders;
   524	        private final boolean isNoEntityStatus;
   525	        private final Consumer<ServerResponseTrailers> beforeTrailers;
   526	
   527	        private BlockingOutputStream(ServerResponseHeaders headers,
   528	                                     WritableHeaders<?> trailers,
   529	                                     Consumer<ServerResponseTrailers> beforeTrailers,
   530	                                     Supplier<Status> status,
   531	                                     Supplier<String> streamResult,
   532	                                     DataWriter dataWriter,
   533	                                     Runnable responseCloseRunnable,
   534	                                     ConnectionContext ctx,
   535	                                     Http1ConnectionListener sendListener,
   536	                                     Http1ServerRequest request,
   537	                                     boolean keepAlive,
   538	                                     boolean validateHeaders,
   539	                                     boolean isNoEntityStatus) {
   540	            this.headers = headers;
   541	            this.trailers = trailers;
   542	            this.beforeTrailers = beforeTrailers;
   543	            this.status = status;
   544	            this.streamResult = streamResult;
   545	            this.dataWriter = dataWriter;
   546	            this.responseCloseRunnable = responseCloseRunnable;
   547	            this.ctx = ctx;
   548	            this.sendListener = sendListener;
   549	            this.contentLength = headers.contentLength().orElse(-1);
   550	            this.request = request;
   551	            this.keepAlive = keepAlive;
   552	            this.validateHeaders = validateHeaders;
   553	            this.isNoEntityStatus = isNoEntityStatus;
   554	        }
   555	
   556	        void checkResponseHeaders() {
   557	            if (headers.contains(HeaderNames.TRAILER)) {
   558	                headers.remove(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH);
   559	                isChunked = true;
   560	                forcedChunked = true;
   561	            } else {
   562	                isChunked = !headers.contains(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH);
   563	                forcedChunked = headers.contains(HeaderValues.TRANSFER_ENCODING_CHUNKED);
   564	            }
   565	        }
   566	
   567	        @Override
   568	        public void write(int b) throws IOException {
   569	            write(BufferData.create(1).write(b));
   570	        }
   571	
   572	        @Override
   573	        public void write(byte[] b) throws IOException {
   574	            write(BufferData.create(b));
   575	        }
   576	
   577	        @Override
   578	        public void write(byte[] b, int off, int len) throws IOException {
   579	            write(BufferData.create(b, off, len));
   580	        }
   581	
   582	        /**
   583	         * Last call to flush before closing should be ignored to properly
   584	         * support content length optimization.
   585	         *
   586	         * @throws IOException an I/O exception
   587	         */
   588	        @Override
   589	        public void flush() throws IOException {
   590	            if (closing) {
   591	                return;     // ignore final flush
   592	            }
   593	            if (firstByte && firstBuffer != null) {
   594	                write(BufferData.empty());
   595	            }
   596	        }
   597	
   598	        /**
   599	         * This is a noop, even when user closes the output stream, we wait for the
   600	         * call to {@link this#commit()}.
   601	         */
   602	        @Override
   603	        public void close() {
   604	            // no-op
   605	        }
   606	
   607	        /**
   608	         * Informs output stream that closing phase has started. Special handling
   609	         * for {@link this#flush()}.
   610	         */
   611	        public void closing() {
   612	            closing = true;
   613	        }
   614	
   615	        void commit() {
   616	            if (closed) {
   617	                return;
   618	            }
   619	            this.closed = true;
   620	            boolean sendTrailers =
   621	                    (isChunked || forcedChunked)
   622	                    && (request.headers().contains(HeaderValues.TE_TRAILERS)
   623	                                || headers.contains(HeaderNames.TRAILER));
   624	
   625	            if (firstByte) {
   626	                if (forcedChunked && firstBuffer != null) {
   627	                    // no sense in sending no data, only do this if chunked requested through a header
   628	                    sendHeadersAndPrepare();
   629	                    writeChunked(firstBuffer);
   630	                    terminatingChunk(sendTrailers);
   631	                } else {
   632	                    sendFirstChunkOnly();
   633	                }
   634	            } else if (isChunked) {
   635	                terminatingChunk(sendTrailers);
   636	            }
   637	
   638	            if (sendTrailers) {
   639	                // not optimized, trailers enabled: we need to write trailers
   640	                trailers.set(STREAM_RESULT_NAME, streamResult.get());
   641	                if (beforeTrailers != null) {
   642	                    beforeTrailers.accept(ServerResponseTrailers.wrap(trailers));
   643	                }
   644	                BufferData buffer = BufferData.growing(128);
   645	                writeHeaders(trailers, buffer, this.validateHeaders);
   646	                buffer.write('\r');        // "\r\n" - empty line after headers
   647	                buffer.write('\n');
   648	                dataWriter.write(buffer);
   649	            }
   650	
   651	            responseCloseRunnable.run();
   652	            try {
   653	                super.close();
   654	            } catch (IOException e) {
   655	                throw new ServerConnectionException("Failed to close server response stream.", e);
   656	            }
   657	        }
   658	
   659	        long totalBytesWritten() {
   660	            return responseBytesTotal;
   661	        }
   662	
   663	        /**
   664	         * Send terminating chunk without trailers {@code  "0\r\n\r\n"} or when trailers are expected {@code  "0\r\n"}.
   665	         *
   666	         * <pre>{@code
   667	         *   chunked-body    = *chunk
   668	         *                     last-chunk
   669	         *                     trailer-section
   670	         *                     CRLF
   671	         *
   672	         *   chunk           = chunk-size [ chunk-ext ] CRLF
   673	         *                     chunk-data CRLF
   674	         *   last-chunk      = 1*("0") [ chunk-ext ] CRLF
   675	         *   trailer-section = *( field-line CRLF )
   676	         *   }</pre>
   677	         *
   678	         * @param trailers whether trailers are expected or not
   679	         * @see <a href="https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9112#section-7.1">rfc9112 §7.1</a>
   680	         */
   681	        private void terminatingChunk(boolean trailers) {
   682	            BufferData terminatingChunk = BufferData.create(trailers ? TERMINATING_CHUNK_TRAILERS : TERMINATING_CHUNK);
   683	            sendListener.data(ctx, terminatingChunk);
   684	            dataWriter.write(terminatingChunk);
   685	        }
   686	
   687	        private void write(BufferData buffer) throws IOException {
   688	            if (closed) {
   689	                throw new IOException("Stream already closed");
   690	            }
   691	            if (isNoEntityStatus && buffer.available() > 0) {
   692	                throw new IllegalStateException("Attempting to write data on a response with status " + status);
   693	            }
   694	
   695	            if (!isChunked) {
   696	                if (firstByte) {
   697	                    firstByte = false;
   698	                    Status usedStatus = status.get();
   699	                    sendListener.status(ctx, usedStatus);
   700	                    sendListener.headers(ctx, headers);
   701	                    // write headers and payload part in one buffer to avoid TCP/ACK delay problems
   702	                    BufferData growing = BufferData.growing(256 + buffer.available());
   703	                    nonEntityBytes(headers, usedStatus, growing, keepAlive, validateHeaders);
   704	                    // check not exceeding content-length
   705	                    bytesWritten += buffer.available();
   706	                    checkContentLength(buffer);
   707	                    sendListener.data(ctx, buffer);
   708	                    // write single buffer headers and payload part
   709	                    growing.write(buffer);
   710	                    responseBytesTotal += growing.available();
   711	                    dataWriter.write(growing);
   712	                } else {
   713	                    // if not chunked, always write
   714	                    writeContent(buffer);
   715	                }
   716	                return;
   717	            }
   718	
   719	            // try chunked data optimization
   720	            if (firstByte && firstBuffer == null) {
   721	                // if somebody re-uses the byte buffer sent to us, we must copy it
   722	                firstBuffer = buffer.copy();
   723	                return;
   724	            }
   725	
   726	            if (firstByte) {
   727	                if (request.headers().contains(HeaderValues.TE_TRAILERS)) {
   728	                    // proper stream with multiple buffers, write status amd headers
   729	                    headers.add(STREAM_TRAILERS);
   730	                }
   731	                // this is chunked encoding, if anybody managed to set content length, it would break everything
   732	                if (headers.contains(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH)
   733	                        && (isNoEntityStatus || buffer.available() > 0)) {
   734	                    LOGGER.log(System.Logger.Level.WARNING, "Content length was set after stream was requested, "
   735	                            + "the response is already chunked, cannot use content-length");
   736	                    headers.remove(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH);
   737	                }
   738	                sendHeadersAndPrepare();
   739	                firstByte = false;
   740	                BufferData combined = BufferData.create(firstBuffer, buffer);
   741	                writeChunked(combined);
   742	                firstBuffer = null;
   743	            } else {
   744	                writeChunked(buffer);
   745	            }
   746	        }
   747	
   748	        private void sendFirstChunkOnly() {
   749	            int contentLength;
   750	            if (firstBuffer == null) {
   751	                headers.set(HeaderValues.CONTENT_LENGTH_ZERO);
   752	                contentLength = 0;
   753	            } else {
   754	                headers.set(HeaderValues.create(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH, String.valueOf(firstBuffer.available())));
   755	                contentLength = firstBuffer.available();
   756	            }
   757	            isChunked = false;
   758	            headers.remove(HeaderNames.TRANSFER_ENCODING);
   759	
   760	            // at this moment, we must send headers
   761	            Status usedStatus = status.get();
   762	            sendListener.status(ctx, usedStatus);
   763	            sendListener.headers(ctx, headers);
   764	            BufferData bufferData = BufferData.growing(contentLength + 256);
   765	            nonEntityBytes(headers, usedStatus, bufferData, keepAlive, validateHeaders);
   766	
   767	            if (firstBuffer != null) {
   768	                bufferData.write(firstBuffer);
   769	            }
   770	
   771	            sendListener.data(ctx, bufferData);
   772	            responseBytesTotal += bufferData.available();
   773	            dataWriter.write(bufferData);
   774	        }
   775	
   776	        private void sendHeadersAndPrepare() {
   777	            if (headers.contains(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH)) {
   778	                contentLength = headers.contentLength().orElse(-1);
   779	                isChunked = false;
   780	            } else {
   781	                contentLength = -1;
   782	                // Add chunked encoding, if there is no other transfer-encoding headers
   783	                if (!headers.contains(HeaderNames.TRANSFER_ENCODING)) {
   784	                    headers.set(HeaderValues.TRANSFER_ENCODING_CHUNKED);
   785	                } else {
   786	                    // Add chunked encoding, if it's not part of existing transfer-encoding headers
   787	                    if (!headers.contains(HeaderValues.TRANSFER_ENCODING_CHUNKED)) {
   788	                        headers.add(HeaderValues.TRANSFER_ENCODING_CHUNKED);
   789	                    }
   790	                }
   791	            }
   792	
   793	            // at this moment, we must send headers
   794	            Status usedStatus = status.get();
   795	            sendListener.status(ctx, usedStatus);
   796	            sendListener.headers(ctx, headers);
   797	            BufferData bufferData = BufferData.growing(256);
   798	            nonEntityBytes(headers, usedStatus, bufferData, keepAlive, validateHeaders);
   799	            sendListener.data(ctx, bufferData);
   800	            responseBytesTotal += bufferData.available();
   801	            dataWriter.write(bufferData);
   802	        }
   803	
   804	        private void writeChunked(BufferData buffer) {
   805	            int available = buffer.available();
   806	            byte[] hex = Integer.toHexString(available).getBytes(StandardCharsets.US_ASCII);
   807	
   808	            BufferData toWrite = BufferData.create(available + hex.length + 4); // \r\n after size, another after chunk
   809	            toWrite.write(hex);
   810	            toWrite.write('\r');
   811	            toWrite.write('\n');
   812	            toWrite.write(buffer);
   813	            toWrite.write('\r');
   814	            toWrite.write('\n');
   815	
   816	            sendListener.data(ctx, toWrite);
   817	            responseBytesTotal += toWrite.available();
   818	            dataWriter.write(toWrite);
   819	        }
   820	
   821	        private void checkContentLength(BufferData ignored) throws IOException {
   822	            if (bytesWritten > contentLength && contentLength != -1) {
   823	                throw new IOException("Content length was set to " + contentLength
   824	                        + ", but you are writing additional " + (bytesWritten - contentLength) + " "
   825	                        + "bytes");
   826	            }
   827	        }
   828	
   829	        private void writeContent(BufferData buffer) throws IOException {
   830	            bytesWritten += buffer.available();
   831	            checkContentLength(buffer);
   832	            sendListener.data(ctx, buffer);
   833	            responseBytesTotal += buffer.available();
   834	            dataWriter.write(buffer);
   835	        }
   836	    }
   837	
   838	    /**
   839	     * A special stream that provides buffering for a delegate and special handling
   840	     * of close logic. Note that due to some locking issues in the JDK, this class
   841	     * must use delegation with {@link BufferedOutputStream} instead of subclassing.
   842	     *
   843	     * <p>If the buffer size is less or equal to zero, it will not wrap the
   844	     * {@link io.helidon.webserver.http1.Http1ServerResponse.BlockingOutputStream}
   845	     * with a {@link java.io.BufferedOutputStream}.
   846	     */
   847	    static class ClosingBufferedOutputStream extends OutputStream {
   848	
   849	        private final BlockingOutputStream closingDelegate;
   850	        private final OutputStream delegate;
   851	
   852	        ClosingBufferedOutputStream(BlockingOutputStream out, int size) {
   853	            this.closingDelegate = out;
   854	            this.delegate = size <= 0 ? out : new BufferedOutputStream(out, size);
   855	        }
   856	
   857	        @Override
   858	        public void write(int b) throws IOException {
   859	            delegate.write(b);
   860	        }
   861	
   862	        @Override
   863	        public void write(byte[] b) throws IOException {
   864	            delegate.write(b);
   865	        }
   866	
   867	        @Override
   868	        public void write(byte[] b, int off, int len) throws IOException {
   869	            delegate.write(b, off, len);
   870	        }
   871	
   872	        @Override
   873	        public void flush() throws IOException {
   874	            delegate.flush();
   875	        }
   876	
   877	        @Override
   878	        public void close() {
   879	            closingDelegate.closing();     // inform of imminent call to close for last flush
   880	            try {
   881	                delegate.close();
   882	            } catch (IOException | UncheckedIOException e) {
   883	                throw new ServerConnectionException("Failed to close server output stream", e);
   884	            }
   885	        }
   886	
   887	        long totalBytesWritten() {
   888	            return closingDelegate.totalBytesWritten();
   889	        }
   890	
   891	        void commit() {
   892	            try {
   893	                flush();
   894	                closingDelegate.commit();
   895	            } catch (IOException | UncheckedIOException e) {
   896	                throw new ServerConnectionException("Failed to flush server output stream", e);
   897	            }
   898	        }
   899	    }
   900	}

    17	package io.helidon.common.socket;
    18	
    19	import java.util.concurrent.ExecutorService;
    20	
    21	import io.helidon.common.buffers.BufferData;
    22	import io.helidon.common.buffers.DataWriter;
    23	
    24	/**
    25	 * Socket writer (possibly) used from multiple threads, takes care of writing to a single
    26	 * socket.
    27	 */
    28	public abstract class SocketWriter implements DataWriter {
    29	    private final HelidonSocket socket;
    30	
    31	    /**
    32	     * A new socket writer.
    33	     *
    34	     * @param socket socket to write to
    35	     */
    36	    protected SocketWriter(HelidonSocket socket) {
    37	        this.socket = socket;
    38	    }
    39	
    40	    /**
    41	     * Create a new socket writer.
    42	     *
    43	     * @param executor         executor used to create a thread for asynchronous writes
    44	     * @param socket           socket to write to
    45	     * @param writeQueueLength maximal number of queued writes, write operation will block if the queue is full; if set to
    46	     *                         {code 1} or lower, write queue is disabled and writes are direct to socket (blocking)
    47	     * @param smartAsyncWrites flag to enable smart async writes, see {@link io.helidon.common.socket.SmartSocketWriter}
    48	     * @return a new socket writer
    49	     */
    50	    public static SocketWriter create(ExecutorService executor,
    51	                                      HelidonSocket socket,
    52	                                      int writeQueueLength,
    53	                                      boolean smartAsyncWrites) {
    54	        if (writeQueueLength <= 1) {
    55	            return new SocketWriterDirect(socket);
    56	        } else {
    57	            return smartAsyncWrites
    58	                    ? new SmartSocketWriter(executor, socket, writeQueueLength)
    59	                    : new SocketWriterAsync(executor, socket, writeQueueLength);
    60	        }
    61	    }
    62	
    63	    /**
    64	     * Create a new socket writer.
    65	     *
    66	     * @param socket           socket to write to
    67	     * @return a new socket writer
    68	     */
    69	    public static SocketWriter create(HelidonSocket socket) {
    70	        return new SocketWriterDirect(socket);
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    @Override
    74	    public void writeNow(BufferData... buffers) {
    75	        BufferData composite = BufferData.create(buffers);
    76	        writeNow(composite);
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    @Override
    80	    public void writeNow(BufferData buffer) {
    81	        socket.write(buffer);
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    /**
    85	     * Close this writer. Will attempt to write all enqueued buffers and will stop the thread if created.
    86	     * Does not close the socket.
    87	     */
    88	    public void close() {
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    /**
    92	     * Provides access to the underlying socket.
    93	     *
    94	     * @return socket
    95	     */
    96	    protected HelidonSocket socket() {
    97	        return socket;
    98	    }
    99	}

    17	package io.helidon.common.socket;
    18	
    19	import java.util.concurrent.ExecutorService;
    20	
    21	import io.helidon.common.buffers.BufferData;
    22	
    23	/**
    24	 * A special socket write that starts async but may switch to sync mode if it
    25	 * detects that the async queue size is below {@link #QUEUE_SIZE_THRESHOLD}.
    26	 * If it switches to sync mode, it shall never return back to async mode.
    27	 */
    28	public class SmartSocketWriter extends SocketWriter {
    29	    private static final long WINDOW_SIZE = 1000;
    30	    private static final double QUEUE_SIZE_THRESHOLD = 2.0;
    31	
    32	    private final SocketWriterAsync asyncWriter;
    33	    private volatile long windowIndex;
    34	    private volatile boolean asyncMode;
    35	
    36	    SmartSocketWriter(ExecutorService executor, HelidonSocket socket, int writeQueueLength) {
    37	        super(socket);
    38	        this.asyncWriter = new SocketWriterAsync(executor, socket, writeQueueLength);
    39	        this.asyncMode = true;
    40	        this.windowIndex = 0L;
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    @Override
    44	    public void write(BufferData... buffers) {
    45	        for (BufferData buffer : buffers) {
    46	            write(buffer);
    47	        }
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    @Override
    51	    public void write(BufferData buffer) {
    52	        if (asyncMode) {
    53	            asyncWriter.write(buffer);
    54	            if (++windowIndex % WINDOW_SIZE == 0 && asyncWriter.avgQueueSize() < QUEUE_SIZE_THRESHOLD) {
    55	                asyncMode = false;
    56	            }
    57	        } else {
    58	            asyncWriter.drainQueue();
    59	            writeNow(buffer);       // blocking write
    60	        }
    61	    }
    62	}

    24

    29	/**
    30	 * Socket writer (possibly) used from multiple threads, takes care of writing to a single
    31	 * socket.
    32	 */
    33	class SocketWriterAsync extends SocketWriter implements DataWriter {
    34	    private static final System.Logger LOGGER = System.getLogger(SocketWriterAsync.class.getName());
    35	    private static final BufferData CLOSING_TOKEN = BufferData.empty();
    36	
    37	    private final ExecutorService executor;
    38	    private final ArrayBlockingQueue<BufferData> writeQueue;
    39	    private final CountDownLatch cdl = new CountDownLatch(1);
    40	    private final AtomicBoolean started = new AtomicBoolean(false);
    41	    private volatile Throwable caught;

    44	    private double avgQueueSize;

    50	     * @param socket           socket to write to
    51	     * @param writeQueueLength maximal number of queued writes, write operation will block if the queue is full; if set to
    52	     *                         {code 1} or lower, write queue is disabled and writes are direct to socket (blocking)
    53	     */
    54	    SocketWriterAsync(ExecutorService executor, HelidonSocket socket, int writeQueueLength) {
    55	        super(socket);
    56	        this.executor = executor;
    57	        this.writeQueue = new ArrayBlockingQueue<>(writeQueueLength);
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    @Override
    61	    public void write(BufferData... buffers) {
    62	        for (BufferData buffer : buffers) {
    63	            write(buffer);
    64	        }
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    @Override
    68	    public void write(BufferData buffer) {
    69	        checkRunning();
    70	        try {
    71	            if (!writeQueue.offer(buffer, 10, TimeUnit.SECONDS)) {
    72	                checkRunning();
    73	                throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to write data to queue, timed out");
    74	            }
    75	        } catch (InterruptedException e) {
    76	            throw new IllegalStateException("Interrupted while trying to write to a queue", e);
    77	        }
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    /**
    81	     * Close this writer. Will attempt to write all enqueued buffers and will stop the thread if created.
    82	     */
    83	    public void close() {
    84	        run = false;
    85	        if (!started.get()) {
    86	            // thread never started
    87	            return;
    88	        }
    89	        try {
    90	            writeQueue.put(CLOSING_TOKEN); // wake up blocked take() operation
    91	            if (cdl.await(1000, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS)) {
    92	                // reads finished because we set run to false
    93	                BufferData available;
    94	                while ((available = writeQueue.poll()) != null) {
    95	                    try {
    96	                        writeNow(available);
    97	                    } catch (Exception e) {
    98	                        LOGGER.log(System.Logger.Level.TRACE, "Failed to write last buffers during writer shutdown", e);
    99	                        // in case we fail to write to socket when closing, it is probably because it is already closed
   100	                        // we still need to release all buffers
   101	                    }
   102	                }
   103	            }
   104	            if (thread != null) {
   105	                // fail blocked writers
   106	                thread.interrupt();
   107	            }
   108	        } catch (InterruptedException e) {            // failed to get
   109	        }
   110	
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    private void run() {
   114	        this.thread = Thread.currentThread();
   115	        this.thread.setName("[" + socket().socketId() + " " + socket().childSocketId() + "]");
   116	        try {
   117	            while (run) {
   118	                CompositeBufferData toWrite = BufferData.createComposite(writeQueue.take());  // wait if the queue is empty
   119	                // we only want to read a certain amount of data, if somebody writes huge amounts
   120	                // we could spin here forever and run out of memory
   121	                int queueSize = 1;
   122	                for (; queueSize <= 1000; queueSize++) {
   123	                    BufferData newBuf = writeQueue.poll(); // drain ~all elements from the queue, don't wait.
   124	                    if (newBuf == null) {
   125	                        break;
   126	                    }
   127	                    toWrite.add(newBuf);
   128	                }
   129	                writeNow(toWrite);
   130	                avgQueueSize = (avgQueueSize + queueSize) / 2.0;
   131	            }
   132	            cdl.countDown();
   133	        } catch (Throwable e) {
   134	            this.caught = e;
   135	            this.run = false;
   136	        }
   137	    }
   138	
   139	    private void checkRunning() {
   140	        if (started.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
   141	            // start writer on first asynchronous write
   142	            executor.submit(this::run);
   143	        }
   144	        if (!run) {
   145	            throw new SocketWriterException(caught);
   146	        }
   147	    }
   148	
   149	    void drainQueue() {
   150	        BufferData buffer;
   151	        while ((buffer = writeQueue.poll()) != null) {
   152	            writeNow(buffer);
   153	        }
   154	    }
   155	
   156	    double avgQueueSize() {
   157	        return avgQueueSize;
   158	    }
   159	}

    28	
    29	/**
    30	 * Plain socket based on NIO {@link java.nio.channels.SocketChannel}.
    31	 * This socket uses ByteBuffer for reading and writing.
    32	 */
    33	public sealed class NioSocket implements HelidonSocket permits TlsNioSocket {
    34	    private static final int BUFFER_LENGTH = 8 * 1024;
    35	
    36	    private final ByteBuffer readBuffer = ByteBuffer.allocate(BUFFER_LENGTH);
    37	    private final ByteBuffer writeBuffer = ByteBuffer.allocate(BUFFER_LENGTH);
    38	
    39	    private final SocketChannel delegate;
    40	    private final String childSocketId;
    41	    private final String socketId;
    42	
    43	    /**
    44	     * Plain socket.
    45	     *
    46	     * @param delegate      delegate socket
    47	     * @param childSocketId channel id
    48	     * @param socketId      server channel id
    49	     */
    50	    protected NioSocket(SocketChannel delegate, String childSocketId, String socketId) {
    51	        this.delegate = delegate;
    52	        this.childSocketId = childSocketId;
    53	        this.socketId = socketId;
    54	    }
    55	
    56	    /**
    57	     * Create a new server socket.
    58	     *
    59	     * @param delegate        underlying socket
    60	     * @param channelId       channel id
    61	     * @param serverChannelId server channel id
    62	     * @return a new plain socket
    63	     */
    64	    public static NioSocket server(SocketChannel delegate, String channelId, String serverChannelId) {
    65	        return new NioSocket(delegate, channelId, serverChannelId);
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    /**
    69	     * Create a new client socket.
    70	     *
    71	     * @param delegate  underlying socket
    72	     * @param channelId channel id
    73	     * @return a new plain socket
    74	     */
    75	    public static NioSocket client(SocketChannel delegate, String channelId) {
    76	        return new NioSocket(delegate, channelId, "client");
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    @Override
    80	    public PeerInfo remotePeer() {
    81	        return PeerInfoImpl.createRemote(this);
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    @Override
    85	    public PeerInfo localPeer() {
    86	        return PeerInfoImpl.createLocal(this);
    87	    }
    88	
    89	    @Override
    90	    public boolean isSecure() {
    91	        return false;
    92	    }
    93

    97	    }
    98	
    99	    @Override

   102	    }
   103	
   104	    @Override
   105	    public void close() {
   106	        try {
   107	            // if close() is called without shutdownOutput(), the remote sometimes does not receive last bytes sent
   108	            delegate.shutdownOutput();
   109	            delegate.shutdownInput();
   110	            delegate.close();
   111	        } catch (IOException e) {
   112	            throw new UncheckedIOException(e);
   113	        }
   114	    }
   115	
   116	    @Override
   117	    public void idle() {
   118	    }
   119	
   120	    @Override
   121	    public boolean isConnected() {
   122	        return delegate.isOpen();
   123	    }
   124	
   125	    @SuppressWarnings("removal")
   126	    @Override
   127	    public int read(BufferData buffer) {
   128	        try {
   129	            if (readBuffer.remaining() == 0) {
   130	                readBuffer.clear();
   131	                delegate.read(readBuffer);
   132	                readBuffer.flip();
   133	            }
   134	            return buffer.readFrom(readBuffer);
   135	        } catch (IOException e) {
   136	            throw new UncheckedIOException(e);
   137	        }
   138	    }
   139	
   140	    @Override
   141	    public void write(BufferData buffer) {
   142	        try {
   143	            while (!buffer.consumed()) {
   144	                writeBuffer.clear();
   145	                buffer.writeTo(writeBuffer, buffer.available());
   146	                writeBuffer.flip();
   147	                delegate.write(writeBuffer);
   148	            }
   149	        } catch (IOException e) {
   150	            throw new UncheckedIOException(e);
   151	        }
   152	    }
   153	
   154	    @Override
   155	    public byte[] get() {
   156	        try {
   157	            int r = delegate.read(readBuffer);
   158	            readBuffer.flip();
   159	            if (r == -1) {
   160	                return null; // end of data
   161	            }
   162	            if (r == 0) {
   163	                throw new IllegalStateException("Read 0 bytes, this should never happen with blocking socket");
   164	            }
   165	            byte[] result = new byte[r];
   166	            readBuffer.get(result);
   167	            return result;
   168	        } catch (IOException e) {
   169	            throw new UncheckedIOException(e);
   170	        } finally {
   171	            readBuffer.clear();
   172	        }
   173	    }
   174	
   175	    /**
   176	     * Write to the underlying socket/channel from the provided buffer.
   177	     * The buffer is not flipped.
   178	     *
   179	     * @param buffer buffer to write
   180	     * @return number of bytes written
   181	     */
   182	    protected int write(ByteBuffer buffer) {
   183	        try {
   184	            return delegate.write(buffer);
   185	        } catch (IOException e) {
   186	            throw new UncheckedIOException(e);
   187	        }
   188	    }
   189	
   190	    /**
   191	     * Read from the underlying socket/channel into the provided buffer.
   192	     * The buffer is not flipped.
   193	     *
   194	     * @param buffer buffer to read to
   195	     * @return number of bytes read
   196	     */
   197	    protected int read(ByteBuffer buffer) {
   198	        try {
   199	            return delegate.read(buffer);
   200	        } catch (IOException e) {
   201	            throw new UncheckedIOException(e);
   202	        }
   203	    }
   204	
   205	    SocketAddress localSocketAddress() {
   206	        try {
   207	            return delegate.getLocalAddress();
   208	        } catch (IOException e) {
   209	            return null;
   210	        }
   211	    }
   212	
   213	    SocketAddress remoteSocketAddress() {
   214	        try {
   215	            return delegate.getRemoteAddress();
   216	        } catch (IOException e) {
   217	            return null;
   218	        }
   219	    }
   220	
   221	    String localHost() {
   222	        SocketAddress localSocketAddress = localSocketAddress();
   223	        if (localSocketAddress instanceof InetSocketAddress inet) {
   224	            return inet.getHostString();
   225	        }
   226	        if (localSocketAddress instanceof UnixDomainSocketAddress unix) {
   227	            return unix.getPath().toString();
   228	        }
   229	        throw new IllegalStateException("Local host is not a supported socket address. Address: "
   230	                                                + localSocketAddress.getClass().getName());
   231	    }
   232	
   233	    String remoteHost() {
   234	        SocketAddress remoteSocketAddress = remoteSocketAddress();
   235	        if (remoteSocketAddress instanceof InetSocketAddress inet) {
   236	            return inet.getHostString();
   237	        }
   238	        if (remoteSocketAddress instanceof UnixDomainSocketAddress unix) {
   239	            return unix.getPath().toString();
   240	        }
   241	        throw new IllegalStateException("Remote host is not a supported socket address. Address: "
   242	                                                + remoteSocketAddress.getClass().getName());
   243	    }
   244	
   245	    int localPort() {
   246	        SocketAddress localSocketAddress = localSocketAddress();
   247	        if (localSocketAddress instanceof InetSocketAddress inet) {
   248	            return inet.getPort();
   249	        }
   250	        if (localSocketAddress instanceof UnixDomainSocketAddress) {
   251	            return -1;
   252	        }
   253	        throw new IllegalStateException("Local host is not an a supported socket address. Address: "
   254	                                                + localSocketAddress.getClass().getName());
   255	    }
   256	
   257	    int remotePort() {
   258	        SocketAddress remoteSocketAddress = remoteSocketAddress();
   259	        if (remoteSocketAddress instanceof InetSocketAddress inet) {
   260	            return inet.getPort();
   261	        }
   262	        if (remoteSocketAddress instanceof UnixDomainSocketAddress) {
   263	            return -1;
   264	        }
   265	        throw new IllegalStateException("Remote host is not an a supported socket address. Address: "
   266	                                                + remoteSocketAddress.getClass().getName());
   267	    }
   268	}
