    28	/**
    29	 * Wrapper around a byte array.
    30	 */
    31	public interface BufferData {
    32	    /**
    33	     * Empty byte array.
    34	     */
    35	    byte[] EMPTY_BYTES = new byte[0];
    36	
    37	    /**
    38	     * Fixed size buffer data.
    39	     *
    40	     * @param length length of the underlying buffer
    41	     * @return new byte array buffer data
    42	     */
    43	    static BufferData create(int length) {
    44	        return new FixedBufferData(length);
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    /**
    48	     * Fixed size buffer data fully written.
    49	     * @param bytes byte array
    50	     * @return new byte array buffer data with write position moved to the last byte
    51	     */
    52	    static BufferData create(byte[] bytes) {
    53	        return new FixedBufferData(bytes);
    54	    }
    55	
    56	    /**
    57	     * Fixed size buffer data fully written.
    58	     *
    59	     * @param bytes byte array
    60	     * @param position position within the byte array
    61	     * @param length number of bytes from position that contain the data
    62	     * @return new byte array buffer data read to be read
    63	     */
    64	    static BufferData create(byte[] bytes, int position, int length) {
    65	        return new FixedBufferData(bytes, position, length);
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    /**
    69	     * Fixed size buffer data fully written.
    70	     * @param bytes byte array
    71	     * @param offset offset within the byte array
    72	     * @param length length
    73	     * @return new byte array buffer data that are read only
    74	     */
    75	    static BufferData createReadOnly(byte[] bytes, int offset, int length) {
    76	        return new ReadOnlyArrayData(bytes, offset, length);
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    /**
    80	     * Growing buffer data.
    81	     * The buffer will grow when necessary to accommodate more bytes.
    82	     * @param initialLength initial buffer length
    83	     * @return growing buffer data
    84	     */
    85	    static BufferData growing(int initialLength) {
    86	        return new GrowingBufferData(initialLength);
    87	    }
    88	
    89	    /**
    90	     * Buffer data mapping multiple buffers.
    91	     * @param data data to wrap
    92	     * @return composite buffer data
    93	     */
    94	    static BufferData create(BufferData... data) {
    95	        if (data.length == 1) {
    96	            return data[0];
    97	        }
    98	        if (data.length == 0) {
    99	            return BufferUtil.EMPTY_BUFFER;
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        return new CompositeArrayBufferData(data);
   103	    }
   104	
   105	    /**
   106	     * Composite buffer data that are mutable.
   107	     * @return composite buffer
   108	     */
   109	    static CompositeBufferData createComposite() {
   110	        return new CompositeListBufferData();
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    /**
   114	     * Composite buffer data that are mutable with initial value.
   115	     *
   116	     * @param first first buffer to be added to the composite buffer
   117	     * @return composite buffer
   118	     */
   119	    static CompositeBufferData createComposite(BufferData first) {
   120	        return new CompositeListBufferData(first);
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    /**
   124	     * Create composite buffer data from a list.
   125	     *
   126	     * @param data list of buffers to use
   127	     * @return composite buffer
   128	     */
   129	    static BufferData create(List<BufferData> data) {
   130	        if (data.size() == 1) {
   131	            return data.iterator().next();
   132	        }
   133	        if (data.isEmpty()) {
   134	            return BufferUtil.EMPTY_BUFFER;
   135	        }
   136	        return new CompositeListBufferData(data);
   137	    }
   138	
   139	    /**
   140	     * Integer to binary string.
   141	     *
   142	     * @param value integer to print as binary
   143	     * @return binary value
   144	     */
   145	    static String toBinaryString(int value) {
   146	        return BufferUtil.toBinaryString(value);
   147	    }
   148	
   149	    /**
   150	     * Get 31 bits of an integer, ignoring the first bit.
   151	     * @param value integer value (32 bits)
   152	     * @return integer value (31 bits)
   153	     */
   154	    static int toInt31(int value) {
   155	        return value & 0x7FFFFFFF;
   156	    }
   157	
   158	    /**
   159	     * Empty buffer data.
   160	     * @return empty buffer
   161	     */
   162	    static BufferData empty() {
   163	        return BufferUtil.EMPTY_BUFFER;
   164	    }
   165	
   166	    /**
   167	     * Create buffer data from a string.
   168	     * @param stringValue UTF-8 string
   169	     * @return buffer data with bytes of the string
   170	     */
   171	    static BufferData create(String stringValue) {
   172	        Objects.requireNonNull(stringValue);
   173	        if (stringValue.isEmpty()) {
   174	            return empty();
   175	        }
   176	        return create(stringValue.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   177	    }
   178	
   179	    /**
   180	     * Reset read and write position of this buffer.
   181	     * Does not impact length.
   182	     *
   183	     * @return this instance
   184	     */
   185	    BufferData reset();
   186	
   187	    /**
   188	     * Set read position to 0, so others may read the same data from the start.
   189	     *
   190	     * @return this instance
   191	     */
   192	    BufferData rewind();
   193	
   194	    /**
   195	     * Reset read and write position and make the buffer empty.
   196	     * Growing buffer length is set to 0
   197	     *
   198	     * @return this instance
   199	     */
   200	    BufferData clear();
   201	
   202	    /**
   203	     * Write all available bytes of this buffer to the output stream.
   204	     *
   205	     * @param out output stream
   206	     */
   207	    void writeTo(OutputStream out);
   208	
   209	    /**
   210	     * Read bytes from the input stream.
   211	     * Reads at least 1 byte.
   212	     * @param in input stream
   213	     * @return number of bytes read, -1 if the input stream is finished
   214	     */
   215	    int readFrom(InputStream in);
   216	
   217	    /**
   218	     * Read bytes from the provided buffer.
   219	     *
   220	     * @param buf byte buffer with data
   221	     * @return number of bytes read, -1 if the buffer is finished
   222	     */
   223	    int readFrom(ByteBuffer buf);
   224	
   225	    /**
   226	     * Read a single byte from this buffer.
   227	     * @return next byte
   228	     */
   229	    int read();
   230	
   231	    /**
   232	     * Read bytes from this buffer into the provided buffer.
   233	     * @param bytes buffer to write to
   234	     * @return number of bytes actually written to the provided buffer
   235	     */
   236	    default int read(byte[] bytes) {
   237	        return read(bytes, 0, bytes.length);
   238	    }
   239	
   240	    /**
   241	     * Read bytes from this buffer into the provided buffer.
   242	     *
   243	     * @param bytes buffer to write to
   244	     * @param position position in the buffer
   245	     * @param length length that can be written
   246	     * @return actual number of bytes written
   247	     */
   248	    int read(byte[] bytes, int position, int length);
   249	
   250	    /**
   251	     * Do an operation on each byte in this buffer.
   252	     *
   253	     * @param length number of bytes to go through
   254	     * @param consumer function that consumes a byte and returns {@code true} if we should proceed to the next byte
   255	     */
   256	    default void forEach(int length, Function<Byte, Boolean> consumer) {
   257	        for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
   258	            if (!consumer.apply((byte) read())) {
   259	                break;
   260	            }
   261	        }
   262	    }
   263	
   264	    /**
   265	     * Read a UTF-8 string from this buffer.
   266	     *
   267	     * @param length number of bytes to read
   268	     * @return string from the bytes
   269	     */
   270	    default String readString(int length) {
   271	        return readString(length, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
   272	    }
   273	
   274	    /**
   275	     * Read a string from this buffer.
   276	     *
   277	     * @param length number of bytes to read
   278	     * @param charset charset of the string, such as {@link java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets#UTF_8} or {@link java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets#US_ASCII}
   279	     * @return string from the bytes
   280	     */
   281	    String readString(int length, Charset charset);
   282	
   283	    /**
   284	     * Whether this buffer is fully consumed (all available bytes were read).
   285	     * @return if this buffer is consumed
   286	     */
   287	    boolean consumed();
   288	
   289	    /**
   290	     * Read 16-bit integer.
   291	     *
   292	     * @return integer from the next 2 bytes
   293	     */
   294	    default int readInt16() {
   295	        int ch1 = read();
   296	        int ch2 = read();
   297	
   298	        return (ch1 << 8) + ch2;
   299	    }
   300	
   301	    /**
   302	     * Read a 24-bit integer.
   303	     *
   304	     * @return integer from the next 3 bytes
   305	     */
   306	    default int readInt24() {
   307	        int ch1 = read();
   308	        int ch2 = read();
   309	        int ch3 = read();
   310	
   311	        return (ch1 << 16) + (ch2 << 8) + ch3;
   312	    }
   313	
   314	    /**
   315	     * Read 32-bit integer.
   316	     *
   317	     * @return integer from the next 4 bytes
   318	     */
   319	    default int readInt32() {
   320	        int ch1 = read();
   321	        int ch2 = read();
   322	        int ch3 = read();
   323	        int ch4 = read();
   324	
   325	        return (ch1 << 24) + (ch2 << 16) + (ch3 << 8) + ch4;
   326	    }
   327	
   328	    /**
   329	     * Read 32-bit unsigned integer (must be represented as a long, as Java integer is 32-bit signed).
   330	     *
   331	     * @return long from the next 4 bytes
   332	     */
   333	    default long readUnsignedInt32() {
   334	        int ch1 = read();
   335	        int ch2 = read();
   336	        int ch3 = read();
   337	        int ch4 = read();
   338	
   339	        return ((long) ch1 << 24) + ((long) ch2 << 16) + ((long) ch3 << 8) + ch4;
   340	    }
   341	
   342	    /**
   343	     * Read 64-bit long.
   344	     *
   345	     * @return long from the next 8 bytes
   346	     */
   347	    default long readLong() {
   348	        return ((long) read() << 56)
   349	                + ((long) (read() & 255) << 48)
   350	                + ((long) (read() & 255) << 40)
   351	                + ((long) (read() & 255) << 32)
   352	                + ((long) (read() & 255) << 24)
   353	                + ((read() & 255) << 16)
   354	                + ((read() & 255) << 8)
   355	                + ((read() & 255));
   356	    }
   357	
   358	    /**
   359	     * Write 8-bit integer.
   360	     *
   361	     * @param number integer to write as a single byte
   362	     * @return this buffer
   363	     */
   364	    default BufferData writeInt8(int number) {
   365	        return write(number);
   366	    }
   367	
   368	    /**
   369	     * Write 16-bit integer.
   370	     *
   371	     * @param number integer to write as 2 bytes
   372	     * @return this buffer
   373	     */
   374	    default BufferData writeInt16(int number) {
   375	        write((byte) (number >>> 8));
   376	        write((byte) number);
   377	        return this;
   378	    }
   379	
   380	    /**
   381	     * Write 24-bit integer.
   382	     *
   383	     * @param number integer to write as 3 bytes
   384	     * @return this buffer
   385	     */
   386	    default BufferData writeInt24(int number) {
   387	        write((byte) (number >>> 16));
   388	        write((byte) (number >>> 8));
   389	        write((byte) number);
   390	        return this;
   391	    }
   392	
   393	    /**
   394	     * Write 32-bit integer.
   395	     *
   396	     * @param number integer to write as 4 bytes
   397	     * @return this buffer
   398	     */
   399	    default BufferData writeInt32(int number) {
   400	        write((byte) (number >>> 24));
   401	        write((byte) (number >>> 16));
   402	        write((byte) (number >>> 8));
   403	        write((byte) number);
   404	        return this;
   405	    }
   406	
   407	    /**
   408	     * Write 32-bit unsigned integer.
   409	     *
   410	     * @param number long to write as 4 bytes
   411	     * @return this buffer
   412	     */
   413	    default BufferData writeUnsignedInt32(long number) {
   414	        write((byte) (number >>> 24));
   415	        write((byte) (number >>> 16));
   416	        write((byte) (number >>> 8));
   417	        write((byte) number);
   418	        return this;
   419	    }
   420	
   421	    /**
   422	     * Write a byte.
   423	     *
   424	     * @param value value
   425	     * @return this buffer
   426	     */
   427	    BufferData write(int value);
   428	
   429	    /**
   430	     * Write n bytes from this buffer to the provided buffer.
   431	     *
   432	     * @param writeBuffer buffer to write to
   433	     * @param length number of bytes to write
   434	     * @return number of bytes actually written
   435	     */
   436	    int writeTo(ByteBuffer writeBuffer, int length);
   437	
   438	    /**
   439	     * Write the byte array to this buffer.
   440	     *
   441	     * @param bytes byte to write
   442	     */
   443	    default void write(byte[] bytes) {
   444	        write(bytes, 0, bytes.length);
   445	    }
   446	
   447	    /**
   448	     * Write the byte array to this buffer.
   449	     *
   450	     * @param bytes bytes to write
   451	     * @param offset offset within the array
   452	     * @param length number of bytes to write (from the offset)
   453	     */
   454	    void write(byte[] bytes, int offset, int length);
   455	
   456	    /**
   457	     * Write the provided buffer to this buffer.
   458	     * @param toWrite buffer to write
   459	     */
   460	    default void write(BufferData toWrite) {
   461	        write(toWrite, toWrite.available());
   462	    }
   463	
   464	    /**
   465	     * Write n bytes from the provided buffer to this buffer.
   466	     * @param toWrite buffer to write
   467	     * @param length number of bytes to write
   468	     */
   469	    void write(BufferData toWrite, int length);
   470	
   471	    /**
   472	     * HPack integer value (may be 1 or more bytes).
   473	     *
   474	     * @param originalValue value (only bitsOfPrefix are used, bits before that are ignored)
   475	     * @param bitsOfPrefix number of bits significant in the value
   476	     * @return integer value
   477	     */
   478	    default int readHpackInt(int originalValue, int bitsOfPrefix) {
   479	        // significant bits of the value
   480	
   481	        int value = originalValue & (0b11111111 >> (8 - bitsOfPrefix));
   482	        /*
   483	        The value is computed as
   484	        max + (read integer from the next x 7 bits, where next 7 bits are read if the first bit of the octet is 1)
   485	         */
   486	        int max = (1 << bitsOfPrefix) - 1;
   487	        if (value < max) { // 31 is the max number of 5 bits
   488	            // value fits into the prefix, no need to read additional bytes
   489	            // System.out.println("Resolved original value " + Integer.toBinaryString(originalValue) + " to " + value);
   490	            return value;
   491	        }
   492	        //System.out.println("Original value " + Integer.toBinaryString(originalValue) + " has more than one byte, carry on: "
   493	        // + value);
   494	        int shiftBy = 0;
   495	        while (true) {
   496	            int next = read();
   497	            //System.out.println("Read additional byte " + Integer.toBinaryString(next));
   498	            value += (next & 0b01111111) << shiftBy; // add all valid bits to the number and continue next cycle
   499	            shiftBy += 7; // the next iteration must be shifted by 7 additional bits
   500	
   501	            if ((next & 0b10000000) == 0) {
   502	                // last byte
   503	                //System.out.println("Resolved values to " + value);
   504	                return value;
   505	            }
   506	        }
   507	    }
   508	
   509	    /**
   510	     * Write hpack integer to this buffer.
   511	     *
   512	     * @param value the full value we want to write
   513	     * @param prefixedInt value to store in the other bits of the first byte
   514	     * @param bitPrefix bits reserved for our value in the first byte
   515	     * @return this instance
   516	     */
   517	    default BufferData writeHpackInt(int value, int prefixedInt, int bitPrefix) {
   518	        // we do not want possible garbage from wrong value
   519	        int prefixedValue = prefixedInt & (~(0b11111111 >> (8 - bitPrefix)));
   520	
   521	        int max = (1 << bitPrefix) - 1;
   522	        if (value < max) {
   523	            write(value | prefixedValue);
   524	            return this;
   525	        }
   526	        write(max | prefixedValue);
   527	
   528	        // now encode the rest of the value
   529	        int remainingValue = value - max;
   530	        while (true) {
   531	            if (remainingValue < (1 << 7)) {
   532	                write(remainingValue);
   533	                return this;
   534	            }
   535	            // write the seven bits + the first bit to mark this continues
   536	            int toWrite = (remainingValue & 0b01111111) | 0b10000000;
   537	            write(toWrite);
   538	
   539	            // shift to the right by seven bits
   540	            remainingValue = remainingValue >> 7;
   541	        }
   542	    }
   543	
   544	    /**
   545	     * Debug this buffer as binary string.
   546	     *
   547	     * @return binary string debug data (including headers)
   548	     */
   549	    String debugDataBinary();
   550	
   551	    /**
   552	     * Debug this buffer as hex string.
   553	     *
   554	     * @param fullBuffer whether to debug all bytes in this buffer ({@code true}), or only unread bytes {@code false})
   555	     * @return hex debug data (including headers)
   556	     */
   557	    String debugDataHex(boolean fullBuffer);
   558	
   559	    /**
   560	     * Debug the full buffer.
   561	     * @return hex debug data (including headers)
   562	     */
   563	    default String debugDataHex() {
   564	        return debugDataHex(true);
   565	    }
   566	
   567	    /**
   568	     * Copy the underlying data into a new buffer that does not retain any reference.
   569	     * Reads this buffer fully and creates a new instance that is not completed.
   570	     *
   571	     * @return copy of data
   572	     */
   573	    default BufferData copy() {
   574	        byte[] copy = new byte[available()];
   575	        read(copy, 0, available());
   576	        return BufferData.create(copy);
   577	    }
   578	
   579	    /**
   580	     * Number of bytes available for reading.
   581	     *
   582	     * @return available bytes
   583	     */
   584	    int available();
   585	
   586	    /**
   587	     * Skip the next n bytes (move read position).
   588	     * @param length number of bytes to skip
   589	     */
   590	    void skip(int length);
   591	
   592	    /**
   593	     * Find index of the provided byte from the current position.
   594	     *
   595	     * @param aByte byte to find
   596	     * @return index of the byte, or {@code -1} if not found
   597	     */
   598	    int indexOf(byte aByte);
   599	
   600	    /**
   601	     * Find last index of the provided byte from the current position.
   602	     *
   603	     * @param aByte byte to find
   604	     * @return index of the byte, or {@code -1} if not found
   605	     */
   606	    default int lastIndexOf(byte aByte) {
   607	        return lastIndexOf(aByte, available());
   608	    }
   609	
   610	    /**
   611	     * Find last index of the provided byte from the current position.
   612	     *
   613	     * @param aByte byte to find
   614	     * @param length maximal length to search for (e.g. this will be the last byte before reaching the length)
   615	     * @return index of the byte, or {@code -1} if not found
   616	     */
   617	    int lastIndexOf(byte aByte, int length);
   618	
   619	    /**
   620	     * Trim the last x bytes from a buffer (remove them).
   621	     *
   622	     * @param x trim by this number of bytes
   623	     * @return this instance
   624	     */
   625	    BufferData trim(int x);
   626	
   627	    /**
   628	     * Number of bytes that can be written to this instance.
   629	     *
   630	     * @return capacity of this buffer
   631	     */
   632	    int capacity();
   633	
   634	    /**
   635	     * Write ascii string to this buffer.
   636	     * @param text ascii string to write
   637	     */
   638	    default void writeAscii(String text) {
   639	        write(text.getBytes(StandardCharsets.US_ASCII));
   640	    }
   641	
   642	    /**
   643	     * Get byte at index (current read position + index).
   644	     * Does not modify any position.
   645	     *
   646	     * @param index index to get
   647	     * @return byte at the index
   648	     */
   649	    int get(int index);
   650	
   651	    /**
   652	     * Read the content of this data as bytes.
   653	     * This method always creates a new byte array.
   654	     *
   655	     * @return byte array with {@link #available()} bytes, may be empty
   656	     */
   657	    default byte[] readBytes() {
   658	        byte[] bytes = new byte[available()];
   659	        read(bytes);
   660	        return bytes;
   661	    }
   662	
   663	    /**
   664	     * Converts this buffer into an {@link java.io.InputStream} that reads
   665	     * all available bytes from the buffer. This method never resets
   666	     * or rewinds the buffer.
   667	     *
   668	     * @return an input stream backed by this buffer
   669	     */
   670	    default InputStream asInputStream() {
   671	        return new InputStream() {
   672	            @Override
   673	            public int read() {
   674	                return BufferData.this.available() > 0 ? BufferData.this.read() : -1;
   675	            }
   676	        };
   677	    }
   678	}

    17	package io.helidon.common.buffers;
    18	
    19	import java.io.InputStream;
    20	import java.io.OutputStream;
    21	import java.nio.ByteBuffer;
    22	import java.nio.charset.Charset;
    23	
    24	class CompositeArrayBufferData extends ReadOnlyBufferData implements CompositeBufferData {
    25	    private final BufferData[] data;
    26	
    27	    CompositeArrayBufferData(BufferData[] data) {
    28	        this.data = data;
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    @Override
    32	    public BufferData rewind() {
    33	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
    34	            datum.rewind();
    35	        }
    36	        return this;
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    @Override
    40	    public void writeTo(OutputStream out) {
    41	        if (data.length == 1) {
    42	            BufferData datum = data[0];
    43	            if (!(datum instanceof CompositeBufferData)) {
    44	                datum.writeTo(out);
    45	                return;
    46	            }
    47	        }
    48	        copy().writeTo(out);
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    @Override
    52	    public int readFrom(InputStream in) {
    53	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
    54	            if (datum.capacity() > 0) {
    55	                return datum.readFrom(in);
    56	            }
    57	        }
    58	        throw new IllegalStateException("The composite buffer is fully written, cannot write additional bytes");
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    @Override
    62	    public int readFrom(ByteBuffer buf) {
    63	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
    64	            if (datum.capacity() > 0) {
    65	                return datum.readFrom(buf);
    66	            }
    67	        }
    68	        throw new IllegalStateException("The composite buffer is fully written, cannot write additional bytes");
    69	    }
    70	
    71	    @Override
    72	    public int read() {
    73	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
    74	            if (!datum.consumed()) {
    75	                return datum.read();
    76	            }
    77	        }
    78	
    79	        throw new ArrayIndexOutOfBoundsException("This buffer has no more bytes");
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    @Override
    83	    public int read(byte[] buffer, int position, int length) {
    84	        int myPosition = position;
    85	        int remaining = length;
    86	
    87	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
    88	            if (datum.available() > 0) {
    89	                int read = datum.read(buffer, myPosition, remaining);
    90	                myPosition += read;
    91	                remaining -= read;
    92	                if (remaining == 0) {
    93	                    break;
    94	                }
    95	            }
    96	        }
    97	
    98	        return myPosition - position;
    99	    }
   100	
   101	    @Override
   102	    public String readString(int length, Charset charset) {
   103	        if (length > available()) {
   104	            throw new ArrayIndexOutOfBoundsException("Requested " + length + " bytes, but only " + available()
   105	                                                             + " were available\n" + debugDataHex(false));
   106	        }
   107	        byte[] buffer = new byte[length];
   108	
   109	        int read = 0;
   110	        int current;
   111	        while (read != length && available() > 0) {
   112	            current = read(buffer, 0, length);
   113	            read += current;
   114	            if (current == 0) {
   115	                throw new IllegalStateException("Read 0 bytes when available: " + available() + "\n" + debugDataHex(false));
   116	            }
   117	        }
   118	        if (read != length) {
   119	            throw new ArrayIndexOutOfBoundsException("Requested " + length + " bytes, but only " + read + " were available");
   120	        }
   121	
   122	        return new String(buffer, charset);
   123	    }
   124	
   125	    @Override
   126	    public boolean consumed() {
   127	        boolean consumed = true;
   128	
   129	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   130	            if (!datum.consumed()) {
   131	                consumed = false;
   132	            }
   133	        }
   134	
   135	        return consumed;
   136	    }
   137	
   138	    @Override
   139	    public int writeTo(ByteBuffer writeBuffer, int limit) {
   140	        int written = 0;
   141	
   142	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   143	            if (datum.consumed()) {
   144	                continue;
   145	            }
   146	            int datumWrote = datum.writeTo(writeBuffer, limit - written);
   147	            if (datumWrote == 0) {
   148	                // not consumed and wrote 0 -> full
   149	                break;
   150	            }
   151	            written += datumWrote;
   152	        }
   153	
   154	        return written;
   155	    }
   156	
   157	    @Override
   158	    public String debugDataBinary() {
   159	        StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
   160	
   161	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   162	            result.append(datum.debugDataBinary());
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        return result.toString();
   166	    }
   167	
   168	    @Override
   169	    public String debugDataHex(boolean fullBuffer) {
   170	        StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
   171	
   172	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   173	            result.append(datum.debugDataHex(fullBuffer));
   174	        }
   175	
   176	        return result.toString();
   177	    }
   178	
   179	    @Override
   180	    public int available() {
   181	        int available = 0;
   182	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   183	            available += datum.available();
   184	        }
   185	        return available;
   186	    }
   187	
   188	    @Override
   189	    public void skip(int length) {
   190	        int remaining = length;
   191	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   192	            int toSkip = Math.min(datum.available(), remaining);
   193	            datum.skip(toSkip);
   194	            remaining -= toSkip;
   195	            if (remaining <= 0) {
   196	                return;
   197	            }
   198	        }
   199	    }
   200	
   201	    @Override
   202	    public int indexOf(byte aByte) {
   203	        int index;
   204	        int indexPrefix = 0;
   205	
   206	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   207	            index = datum.indexOf(aByte);
   208	            if (index > -1) {
   209	                return indexPrefix + index;
   210	            }
   211	            indexPrefix += datum.available();
   212	        }
   213	
   214	        return -1;
   215	    }
   216	
   217	    @Override
   218	    public int lastIndexOf(byte aByte, int length) {
   219	        int index;
   220	        int lengthRemaining = length;
   221	
   222	        for (int i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
   223	            BufferData datum = data[i];
   224	            index = datum.lastIndexOf(aByte, Math.min(lengthRemaining, datum.available()));
   225	            if (index > -1) {
   226	                return index;
   227	            }
   228	            lengthRemaining -= datum.available();
   229	            if (lengthRemaining <= 0) {
   230	                break;
   231	            }
   232	        }
   233	        return -1;
   234	    }
   235	
   236	    @Override
   237	    public BufferData trim(int x) {
   238	        if (available() < x) {
   239	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Trimming more bytes than available");
   240	        }
   241	        int toRemove = x;
   242	        for (int i = data.length - 1; i > -1; i--) {
   243	            if (toRemove == 0) {
   244	                return this;
   245	            }
   246	            BufferData datum = data[i];
   247	            if (datum.available() > 0) {
   248	                int removed = Math.min(datum.available(), toRemove);
   249	                toRemove -= removed;
   250	                datum.trim(removed);
   251	            }
   252	        }
   253	        if (toRemove == 0) {
   254	            return this;
   255	        }
   256	
   257	        throw new IllegalStateException("Could not trim buffer by " + x + " bytes");
   258	    }
   259	
   260	    @Override
   261	    public int get(int index) {
   262	        int inDataIndex = index;
   263	
   264	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   265	            int available = datum.available();
   266	
   267	            if (available <= inDataIndex) {
   268	                inDataIndex -= available;
   269	                continue;
   270	            }
   271	            return datum.get(inDataIndex);
   272	        }
   273	        throw new ArrayIndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid index to get: " + index);
   274	    }
   275	
   276	    @Override
   277	    public String toString() {
   278	        return "comp-array: a=" + available();
   279	    }
   280	
   281	    @Override
   282	    public CompositeBufferData add(BufferData bufferData) {
   283	        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Add not supported for " + getClass().getSimpleName() + " buffer");
   284	    }
   285	}

   165	
   166	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   167	            result.append(datum.debugDataBinary());
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        return result.toString();
   171	    }
   172	
   173	    @Override
   174	    public String debugDataHex(boolean fullBuffer) {
   175	        StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
   176	
   177	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   178	            result.append(datum.debugDataHex(fullBuffer));
   179	        }
   180	
   181	        return result.toString();
   182	    }
   183	
   184	    @Override
   185	    public int available() {
   186	        int available = 0;
   187	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   188	            available += datum.available();
   189	        }
   190	        return available;
   191	    }
   192	
   193	    @Override
   194	    public void skip(int length) {
   195	        int remaining = length;
   196	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   197	            int toSkip = Math.min(datum.available(), remaining);
   198	            datum.skip(toSkip);
   199	            remaining -= toSkip;
   200	            if (remaining <= 0) {
   201	                return;
   202	            }
   203	        }
   204	    }
   205	
   206	    @Override
   207	    public int indexOf(byte aByte) {
   208	        int index;
   209	        int indexPrefix = 0;
   210	
   211	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   212	            index = datum.indexOf(aByte);
   213	            if (index > -1) {
   214	                return indexPrefix + index;
   215	            }
   216	            indexPrefix += datum.available();
   217	        }
   218	
   219	        return -1;
   220	    }
   221	
   222	    @Override
   223	    public int lastIndexOf(byte aByte, int length) {
   224	        int index;
   225	        int lengthRemaining = length;
   226	
   227	        for (int i = data.size() - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
   228	            BufferData datum = data.get(i);
   229	            index = datum.lastIndexOf(aByte, Math.min(lengthRemaining, datum.available()));
   230	            if (index > -1) {
   231	                return index;
   232	            }
   233	            lengthRemaining -= datum.available();
   234	            if (lengthRemaining <= 0) {
   235	                break;
   236	            }
   237	        }
   238	        return -1;
   239	    }
   240	
   241	    @Override
   242	    public BufferData trim(int x) {
   243	        if (available() < x) {
   244	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Trimming more bytes than available");
   245	        }
   246	        int toRemove = x;
   247	        List<BufferData> bufferList = new ArrayList<>(data);
   248	        for (int i = bufferList.size() - 1; i > -1; i--) {
   249	            if (toRemove == 0) {
   250	                return this;
   251	            }
   252	            BufferData datum = bufferList.get(i);
   253	            if (datum.available() > 0) {
   254	                int removed = Math.min(datum.available(), toRemove);
   255	                toRemove -= removed;
   256	                datum.trim(removed);
   257	            }
   258	        }
   259	        if (toRemove == 0) {
   260	            return this;
   261	        }
   262	
   263	        throw new IllegalStateException("Could not trim buffer by " + x + " bytes");
   264	    }
   265	
   266	    @Override
   267	    public int get(int index) {
   268	        int inDataIndex = index;
   269	
   270	        for (BufferData datum : data) {
   271	            int available = datum.available();
   272	
   273	            if (available <= inDataIndex) {
   274	                inDataIndex -= available;
   275	                continue;
   276	            }
   277	            return datum.get(inDataIndex);
   278	        }
   279	        throw new ArrayIndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid index to get: " + index);
   280	    }
   281	
   282	    @Override
   283	    public String toString() {
   284	        return "comp-list: a=" + available();
   285	    }
   286	}

    17	package io.helidon.common.buffers;
    18	
    19	import java.io.IOException;
    20	import java.io.InputStream;
    21	import java.io.OutputStream;
    22	import java.io.UncheckedIOException;
    23	import java.nio.ByteBuffer;
    24	import java.nio.charset.Charset;
    25	
    26	class FixedBufferData implements BufferData {
    27	    private final byte[] bytes;
    28	    private final int length;
    29	    private int writePosition;
    30	    private int readPosition;
    31	
    32	    FixedBufferData(int length) {
    33	        this.bytes = new byte[length];
    34	        this.length = length;
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    FixedBufferData(byte[] bytes) {
    38	        this.bytes = bytes;
    39	        this.length = bytes.length;
    40	        this.writePosition = this.length;
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    FixedBufferData(byte[] bytes, int position, int length) {
    44	        this.bytes = bytes;
    45	        this.length = length;
    46	        this.writePosition = position + length;
    47	        this.readPosition = position;
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    @Override
    51	    public FixedBufferData reset() {
    52	        this.writePosition = 0;
    53	        this.readPosition = 0;
    54	        return this;
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    @Override
    58	    public BufferData rewind() {
    59	        this.readPosition = 0;
    60	        return this;
    61	    }
    62	
    63	    @Override
    64	    public BufferData clear() {
    65	        return reset();
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    @Override
    69	    public void writeTo(OutputStream out) {
    70	        try {
    71	            out.write(bytes, readPosition, writePosition);
    72	            readPosition = writePosition;
    73	        } catch (IOException e) {
    74	            throw new UncheckedIOException(e);
    75	        }
    76	    }
    77	
    78	    @Override
    79	    public int readFrom(InputStream in) {
    80	        int toRead = length - writePosition;
    81	        int read;
    82	        try {
    83	            read = in.read(bytes, writePosition, toRead);
    84	        } catch (IOException e) {
    85	            throw new UncheckedIOException(e);
    86	        }
    87	        if (read == -1) {
    88	            return read;
    89	        }
    90	        writePosition += read;
    91	        return read;
    92	    }
    93	
    94	    @Override
    95	    public int readFrom(ByteBuffer buf) {
    96	        int toRead = length - writePosition;
    97	        int read = Math.min(toRead, buf.remaining());
    98	        buf.get(bytes, writePosition, read);
    99	        writePosition += read;
   100	        return read;
   101	    }
   102	
   103	    @Override
   104	    public int read() {
   105	        if (readPosition >= writePosition) {
   106	            throw new ArrayIndexOutOfBoundsException("This buffer has " + length
   107	                                                             + " bytes, requested to read at " + readPosition);
   108	        }
   109	        return bytes[readPosition++] & 0xFF;
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    @Override
   113	    public int read(byte[] bytes, int position, int length) {
   114	        int available = this.writePosition - readPosition;
   115	        int toRead = Math.min(length, available);
   116	
   117	        System.arraycopy(this.bytes, readPosition, bytes, position, toRead);
   118	
   119	        readPosition += toRead;
   120	        return toRead;
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    @Override
   124	    public String readString(int length, Charset charset) {
   125	        String result = new String(bytes, readPosition, length, charset);
   126	        readPosition += length;
   127	        return result;
   128	    }
   129	
   130	    public boolean consumed() {
   131	        return readPosition == writePosition;
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    public FixedBufferData write(int value) {
   135	        this.bytes[writePosition++] = (byte) value;
   136	        return this;
   137	    }
   138	
   139	    @Override
   140	    public int writeTo(ByteBuffer writeBuffer, int length) {
   141	        int toWrite = Math.min(writeBuffer.limit() - writeBuffer.position(), writePosition - readPosition);
   142	        toWrite = Math.min(toWrite, length);
   143	        if (toWrite == 0) {
   144	            return 0;
   145	        }
   146	        writeBuffer.put(this.bytes, readPosition, toWrite);
   147	        readPosition += toWrite;
   148	        return toWrite;
   149	    }
   150	
   151	    public void write(byte[] bytes, int offset, int length) {
   152	        System.arraycopy(bytes, offset, this.bytes, writePosition, length);
   153	        writePosition += length;
   154	    }
   155	
   156	    @Override
   157	    public void write(BufferData toWrite) {
   158	        byte[] buffer = new byte[length - writePosition];
   159	        int read = toWrite.read(buffer);
   160	        System.arraycopy(buffer, 0, this.bytes, writePosition, read);
   161	        writePosition += read;
   162	    }
   163	
   164	    @Override
   165	    public void write(BufferData toWrite, int length) {
   166	        byte[] buffer = new byte[length];
   167	        int read = toWrite.read(buffer);
   168	        System.arraycopy(buffer, 0, this.bytes, writePosition, read);
   169	        writePosition += read;
   170	    }
   171	
   172	    @Override
   173	    public String debugDataBinary() {
   174	        return BufferUtil.debugDataBinary(bytes, 0, writePosition);
   175	    }
   176	
   177	    @Override
   178	    public String debugDataHex(boolean fullBuffer) {
   179	        if (fullBuffer) {
   180	            return BufferUtil.debugDataHex(bytes, 0, writePosition);
   181	        } else {
   182	            return BufferUtil.debugDataHex(bytes, readPosition, writePosition);
   183	        }
   184	    }
   185	
   186	    @Override
   187	    public int available() {
   188	        return writePosition - readPosition;
   189	    }
   190	
   191	    @Override
   192	    public void skip(int length) {
   193	        readPosition += length;
   194	    }
   195	
   196	    @Override
   197	    public int indexOf(byte aByte) {
   198	        for (int i = readPosition; i < (readPosition + available()); i++) {
   199	            if (aByte == bytes[i]) {
   200	                return i - readPosition;
   201	            }
   202	        }
   203	        return -1;
   204	    }
   205	
   206	    @Override
   207	    public int lastIndexOf(byte aByte, int length) {
   208	        for (int i = (readPosition + length) - 1; i >= readPosition; i--) {
   209	            byte b = bytes[i];
   210	            if (b == aByte) {
   211	                return i - readPosition;
   212	            }
   213	        }
   214	        return -1;
   215	    }
   216	
   217	    @Override
   218	    public BufferData trim(int x) {
   219	        if (available() < x) {
   220	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Trimming more bytes than available");
   221	        }
   222	        writePosition -= x;
   223	        return this;
   224	    }
   225	
   226	    @Override
   227	    public int capacity() {
   228	        return length - writePosition;
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    @Override
   232	    public int get(int index) {
   233	        return bytes[readPosition + index];
   234	    }
   235	
   236	    @Override
   237	    public String toString() {
   238	        return "fixed: l=" + length + ", r=" + readPosition + ", w=" + writePosition;
   239	    }
   240	}

```java
    return written;
}
```

This should work correctly. But let me check the `ReadOnlyArrayData.writeTo`:

```java
public int writeTo(ByteBuffer writeBuffer, int length) {
    int toWrite = Math.min(writeBuffer.limit() - writeBuffer.position(), this.length - this.position);
    toWrite = Math.min(toWrite, length);
    if (toWrite == 0) {
        return 0;
    }
    writeBuffer.put(this.bytes, offset + position, toWrite);
    position += toWrite;
    return toWrite;
}
```

Wait, there's a bug in `ReadOnlyArrayData.writeTo`! Look at:
```java
int toWrite = Math.min(writeBuffer.limit() - writeBuffer.position(), this.length - this.position);
```

But after `clear()`, the writeBuffer has `limit = capacity` and `position = 0`. So `limit - position = capacity`. But what if `writeBuffer` was not cleared? Actually it always is cleared before use in `NioSocket.write()`.

Now, the `CompositeArrayBufferData.writeTo`:
```java
public int writeTo(ByteBuffer writeBuffer, int limit) {
    int written = 0;
    for (BufferData datum : data) {
        if (datum.consumed()) {
            continue;
        }
        int datumWrote = datum.writeTo(writeBuffer, limit - written);
        if (datumWrote == 0) {
            // not consumed and wrote 0 -> full
            break;
        }
        written += datumWrote;
    }
    return written;
}
```

This looks the same as `CompositeListBufferData.writeTo`.

Hmm, let me think about this differently. The PR description mentions:
- "If using chunked transfer, I occasionally see 'missing CR' or 'Malformed encoding found in chunked-encoding'"
- "If sending content-length header, the transfer occasionally just gets stuck completely"

The stack trace shows:
```
Caused by: java.io.UncheckedIOException: java.io.IOException: Broken pipe
    at io.helidon.common.socket.NioSocket.write(NioSocket.java:150)
    at io.helidon.common.socket.SocketWriter.writeNow(SocketWriter.java:81)
    at io.helidon.common.socket.SocketWriterDirect.write(SocketWriterDirect.java:43)
    at io.helidon.webserver.http1.Http1ServerResponse$BlockingOutputStream.writeChunked(Http1ServerResponse.java:818)
```

So the `writeChunked` method is calling `dataWriter.write(toWrite)` which goes through `SocketWriterDirect.write(buffer)` → `SocketWriter.writeNow(buffer)` → `NioSocket.write(buffer)`.

But `SocketWriterDirect` is only used when `writeQueueLength <= 1`. If the server is configured with smart/sync writes, it would use `SmartSocketWriter` or `SocketWriterAsync`.

Let me check how the writer is configured:</think>Let me look for how the `DataWriter` is configured in the HTTP/1.

    73	/**
    74	 * HTTP/1.1 server connection.
    75	 */
    76	public class Http1Connection implements ServerConnection, InterruptableTask<Void> {
    77	    static final byte[] CONTINUE_100 = "HTTP/1.1 100 Continue\r\n\r\n".getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    78	    private static final System.Logger LOGGER = System.getLogger(Http1Connection.class.getName());
    79	    private static final Supplier<RequestException> INVALID_SIZE_EXCEPTION_SUPPLIER =
    80	            () -> RequestException.builder()
    81	                    .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
    82	                    .message("Chunk size is invalid")
    83	                    .build();
    84	    private final ConnectionContext ctx;
    85	    private final Http1Config http1Config;
    86	    private final DataWriter writer;
    87	    private final DataReader reader;
    88	    private final Map<String, Http1Upgrader> upgradeProviderMap;
    89	    private final boolean canUpgrade;
    90	    private final Http1Headers http1headers;
    91	    private final Http1Prologue http1prologue;
    92	    private final ContentEncodingContext contentEncodingContext;
    93	    private final HttpRouting routing;
    94	    private final long maxPayloadSize;
    95	    private final Http1ConnectionListener recvListener;
    96	    private final Http1ConnectionListener sendListener;
    97	
    98	    // overall connection
    99	    private int requestId;
   100	    private long currentEntitySize;
   101	    private long currentEntitySizeRead;
   102	
   103	    private volatile Thread myThread;
   104	    private volatile boolean canRun = true;
   105	    private volatile boolean currentlyReadingPrologue;
   106	    private volatile ZonedDateTime lastRequestTimestamp;
   107	    private volatile ServerConnection upgradeConnection;
   108	
   109	    /**
   110	     * Create a new connection.
   111	     *
   112	     * @param ctx                connection context
   113	     * @param http1Config        connection provider configuration
   114	     * @param upgradeProviderMap map of upgrade providers (protocol id to provider)
   115	     */
   116	    Http1Connection(ConnectionContext ctx,
   117	                    Http1Config http1Config,
   118	                    Map<String, Http1Upgrader> upgradeProviderMap) {
   119	        this.ctx = ctx;
   120	        this.writer = ctx.dataWriter();
   121	        this.reader = ctx.dataReader();
   122	        this.http1Config = http1Config;
   123	        this.upgradeProviderMap = upgradeProviderMap;
   124	        this.canUpgrade = !upgradeProviderMap.isEmpty();
   125	        this.recvListener = http1Config.compositeReceiveListener();
   126	        this.sendListener = http1Config.compositeSendListener();
   127	        this.reader.listener(recvListener, ctx);
   128	        this.http1headers = new Http1Headers(reader, http1Config.maxHeadersSize(), http1Config.validateRequestHeaders());
   129	        this.http1prologue = new Http1Prologue(reader, http1Config.maxPrologueLength(), http1Config.validatePath());
   130	        this.contentEncodingContext = ctx.listenerContext().contentEncodingContext();
   131	        this.routing = ctx.router().routing(HttpRouting.class, HttpRouting.empty());
   132	        this.maxPayloadSize = ctx.listenerContext().config().maxPayloadSize();
   133	        this.lastRequestTimestamp = DateTime.timestamp();
   134	    }
   135	
   136	    @Override
   137	    public boolean canInterrupt() {
   138	        if (upgradeConnection == null) {
   139	            return currentlyReadingPrologue;
   140	        }
   141	        return true;
   142	    }
   143	
   144	    @SuppressWarnings("removal")
   145	    @Override
   146	    public void handle(Limit limit) throws InterruptedException {
   147	        this.myThread = Thread.currentThread();
   148	        try {
   149	            // look for protocol data
   150	            ProxyProtocolData proxyProtocolData = ctx.proxyProtocolData().orElse(null);
   151	
   152	            // handle connection until an exception (or explicit connection close)
   153	            while (canRun) {
   154	                // prologue (first line of request)
   155	                currentlyReadingPrologue = true;
   156	                HttpPrologue prologue = http1prologue.readPrologue();
   157	                currentlyReadingPrologue = false;
   158	                lastRequestTimestamp = DateTime.timestamp();
   159	                recvListener.prologue(ctx, prologue);
   160	                currentEntitySize = 0;
   161	                currentEntitySizeRead = 0;
   162	
   163	                if (http1Config.validatePrologue()) {
   164	                    validatePrologue(prologue);
   165	                }
   166	
   167	                WritableHeaders<?> headers = http1headers.readHeaders(prologue);
   168	                if (http1Config.validateRequestHeaders()) {
   169	                    validateHostHeader(prologue, headers, http1Config.validateRequestHostHeader());
   170	                }
   171	                ctx.remotePeer().tlsCertificates()
   172	                        .flatMap(TlsUtils::parseCn)
   173	                        .ifPresent(name -> headers.set(X_HELIDON_CN, name));
   174	                recvListener.headers(ctx, headers);
   175	
   176	                // proxy protocol related headers X-Forwarded-For and X-Forwarded-Port
   177	                if (proxyProtocolData != null) {
   178	                    String sourceAddress = proxyProtocolData.sourceAddress();
   179	                    if (!sourceAddress.isEmpty()) {
   180	                        headers.add(X_FORWARDED_FOR, sourceAddress);
   181	                    }
   182	                    int sourcePort = proxyProtocolData.sourcePort();
   183	                    if (sourcePort != -1) {
   184	                        headers.add(X_FORWARDED_PORT, sourcePort);
   185	                    }
   186	                }
   187	
   188	                if (canUpgrade && headers.contains(HeaderNames.UPGRADE)) {
   189	                    if (!upgradeHasEntity(headers)) {
   190	                        Http1Upgrader upgrader = upgradeProviderMap.get(headers.get(HeaderNames.UPGRADE).get());
   191	                        if (upgrader != null) {
   192	                            ServerConnection upgradeConnection = upgrader.upgrade(ctx, prologue, headers);
   193	                            // upgrader may decide not to upgrade this connection
   194	                            if (upgradeConnection != null) {
   195	                                if (LOGGER.isLoggable(TRACE)) {
   196	                                    LOGGER.log(TRACE, "Connection upgrade using " + upgradeConnection);
   197	                                }
   198	                                this.upgradeConnection = upgradeConnection;
   199	                                // this will block until the connection terminates
   200	                                upgradeConnection.handle(limit);
   201	                                return;
   202	                            }
   203	                        }
   204	                    } else {
   205	                        ctx.log(LOGGER, DEBUG, "Protocol upgrade for a request with a payload ignored");
   206	                    }
   207	                }
   208	
   209	                LimitAlgorithm.Outcome outcome = limit.tryAcquireOutcome(true);
   210	                if (outcome.disposition() == LimitAlgorithm.Outcome.Disposition.ACCEPTED) {
   211	                    LimitAlgorithm.Outcome.Accepted accepted = (LimitAlgorithm.Outcome.Accepted) outcome;
   212	                    LimitAlgorithm.Token permit = accepted.token();
   213	
   214	                    try {
   215	                        this.lastRequestTimestamp = DateTime.timestamp();
   216	                        route(prologue, headers, accepted);
   217	                        permit.success();
   218	                        this.lastRequestTimestamp = DateTime.timestamp();
   219	                    } catch (Throwable e) {
   220	                        permit.dropped();
   221	                        throw e;
   222	                    }
   223	                } else {
   224	                    ctx.log(LOGGER, TRACE, "Too many concurrent requests, rejecting request and closing connection.");
   225	                    throw RequestException.builder()
   226	                            .setKeepAlive(false)
   227	                            .status(Status.SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE_503)
   228	                            .type(EventType.OTHER)
   229	                            .message("Too Many Concurrent Requests")
   230	                            .build();
   231	                }
   232	            }
   233	        } catch (CloseConnectionException e) {
   234	            throw e;
   235	        } catch (BadRequestException e) {
   236	            handleRequestException(RequestException.builder()
   237	                                           .message(e.getMessage())
   238	                                           .cause(e)
   239	                                           .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   240	                                           .status(e.status())
   241	                                           .build());
   242	        } catch (RequestException e) {
   243	            handleRequestException(e);
   244	        } catch (Throwable e) {
   245	            handleRequestException(RequestException.builder()
   246	                                           .message("Internal error")
   247	                                           .type(EventType.INTERNAL_ERROR)
   248	                                           .cause(e)
   249	                                           .build());
   250	        }
   251	    }
   252	
   253	    @SuppressWarnings("removal")
   254	    @Override
   255	    public void handle(Semaphore requestSemaphore) throws InterruptedException {
   256	        handle(FixedLimit.create(requestSemaphore));
   257	    }
   258	
   259	    @Override
   260	    public Duration idleTime() {
   261	        if (upgradeConnection == null) {
   262	            return Duration.between(lastRequestTimestamp, DateTime.timestamp());
   263	        }
   264	        return upgradeConnection.idleTime();
   265	    }
   266	
   267	    @Override
   268	    public void close(boolean interrupt) {
   269	        ctx.log(LOGGER, TRACE, "Requested connection close, interrupt: %s", interrupt);
   270	        // either way, finish
   271	        this.canRun = false;
   272	
   273	        if (upgradeConnection == null) {
   274	            if (interrupt) {
   275	                // interrupt regardless of current state
   276	                if (myThread != null) {
   277	                    myThread.interrupt();
   278	                }
   279	            } else if (canInterrupt()) {
   280	                // only interrupt when not processing a request (there is a chance of a race condition, this edge case
   281	                // is ignored
   282	                myThread.interrupt();
   283	            }
   284	        } else {
   285	            upgradeConnection.close(interrupt);
   286	        }
   287	    }
   288	
   289	    void reset() {
   290	        currentEntitySize = 0;
   291	        currentEntitySizeRead = 0;
   292	    }
   293	
   294	    /**
   295	     * Only accept protocol upgrades if no entity is present. Otherwise, a successful
   296	     * upgrade may result in the request entity interpreted as part of the new protocol
   297	     * data, resulting in a failure.
   298	     *
   299	     * @param headers the HTTP headers in the prologue
   300	     * @return whether to accept or reject the upgrade
   301	     */
   302	    static boolean upgradeHasEntity(WritableHeaders<?> headers) {
   303	        return headers.contains(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH) && !headers.contains(HeaderValues.CONTENT_LENGTH_ZERO)
   304	                || headers.contains(HeaderValues.TRANSFER_ENCODING_CHUNKED);
   305	    }
   306	
   307	    static void validateHostHeader(HttpPrologue prologue, WritableHeaders<?> headers, boolean fullValidation) {
   308	        if (fullValidation) {
   309	            try {
   310	                doValidateHostHeader(prologue, headers);
   311	            } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
   312	                throw RequestException.builder()
   313	                        .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   314	                        .status(Status.BAD_REQUEST_400)
   315	                        .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   316	                        .setKeepAlive(false)
   317	                        .message("Invalid Host header: " + e.getMessage())
   318	                        .cause(e)
   319	                        .build();
   320	            }
   321	        } else {
   322	            simpleHostHeaderValidation(prologue, headers);
   323	        }
   324	    }
   325	
   326	    private void validatePrologue(HttpPrologue prologue) {
   327	        try {
   328	            // scheme is not validated, as it is fixed and validated by the prologue reader
   329	            UriValidator.validateQuery(prologue.query().rawValue());
   330	            if (prologue.fragment().hasValue()) {
   331	                UriValidator.validateFragment(prologue.fragment().rawValue());
   332	            }
   333	        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
   334	            throw RequestException.builder()
   335	                    .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   336	                    .status(Status.BAD_REQUEST_400)
   337	                    .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, ServerRequestHeaders.create()))
   338	                    .setKeepAlive(false)
   339	                    .message(e.getMessage())
   340	                    .safeMessage(true)
   341	                    .cause(e)
   342	                    .build();
   343	        }
   344	    }
   345	
   346	    private static void simpleHostHeaderValidation(HttpPrologue prologue, WritableHeaders<?> headers) {
   347	        if (headers.contains(HeaderNames.HOST)) {
   348	            String host = headers.get(HeaderNames.HOST).get();
   349	            // this is what is used to set up URI information, and this MUST work
   350	            int index = host.lastIndexOf(':');
   351	            if (index < 1) {
   352	                return;
   353	            }
   354	            // this may still be an IPv6 address
   355	            if (host.charAt(host.length() - 1) == ']') {
   356	                // IP literal without port
   357	                return;
   358	            }
   359	
   360	            try {
   361	                // port must be parseable to int
   362	                Integer.parseInt(host.substring(index + 1));
   363	            } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
   364	                throw RequestException.builder()
   365	                        .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   366	                        .status(Status.BAD_REQUEST_400)
   367	                        .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   368	                        .setKeepAlive(false)
   369	                        .message("Invalid port of the host header: " + HtmlEncoder.encode(host.substring(index + 1)))
   370	                        .build();
   371	            }
   372	
   373	        }
   374	
   375	    }
   376	
   377	    private static void doValidateHostHeader(HttpPrologue prologue, WritableHeaders<?> headers) {
   378	        List<String> hostHeaders = headers.all(HeaderNames.HOST, List::of);
   379	        if (hostHeaders.isEmpty()) {
   380	            throw RequestException.builder()
   381	                    .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   382	                    .status(Status.BAD_REQUEST_400)
   383	                    .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   384	                    .setKeepAlive(false)
   385	                    .message("Host header must be present in the request")
   386	                    .build();
   387	        }
   388	        if (hostHeaders.size() > 1) {
   389	            throw RequestException.builder()
   390	                    .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   391	                    .status(Status.BAD_REQUEST_400)
   392	                    .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   393	                    .setKeepAlive(false)
   394	                    .message("Only a single Host header is allowed in request")
   395	                    .build();
   396	        }
   397	        String host = hostHeaders.getFirst();
   398	        if (host.isEmpty()) {
   399	            throw RequestException.builder()
   400	                    .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   401	                    .status(Status.BAD_REQUEST_400)
   402	                    .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   403	                    .setKeepAlive(false)
   404	                    .message("Host header must not be empty")
   405	                    .build();
   406	        }
   407	        // now host and port must be valid
   408	        int startLiteral = host.indexOf('[');
   409	        int endLiteral = host.lastIndexOf(']');
   410	        if (startLiteral == 0 && endLiteral == host.length() - 1) {
   411	            // this is most likely an IPv6 address without a port
   412	            UriValidator.validateIpLiteral(host);
   413	            return;
   414	        }
   415	        if (startLiteral == 0 && endLiteral == -1) {
   416	            UriValidator.validateIpLiteral(host);
   417	            return;
   418	        }
   419	        int colon = host.lastIndexOf(':');
   420	        if (colon == -1) {
   421	            // only host
   422	            UriValidator.validateNonIpLiteral(host);
   423	            return;
   424	        }
   425	
   426	        String portString = host.substring(colon + 1);
   427	        try {
   428	            Integer.parseInt(portString);
   429	        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
   430	            throw RequestException.builder()
   431	                    .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   432	                    .status(Status.BAD_REQUEST_400)
   433	                    .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   434	                    .setKeepAlive(false)
   435	                    .message("Invalid port of the host header: " + HtmlEncoder.encode(portString))
   436	                    .build();
   437	        }
   438	        String hostString = host.substring(0, colon);
   439	        // can be
   440	        // IP-literal [..::]
   441	        if (startLiteral == 0 && endLiteral == hostString.length() - 1) {
   442	            UriValidator.validateIpLiteral(hostString);
   443	            return;
   444	        }
   445	
   446	        UriValidator.validateNonIpLiteral(hostString);
   447	    }
   448	
   449	    private BufferData readEntityFromPipeline(HttpPrologue prologue, WritableHeaders<?> headers) {
   450	        if (currentEntitySize == -1) {
   451	            // chunked
   452	            return readNextChunk(prologue, headers);
   453	        } else {
   454	            // length
   455	            return readLengthEntity();
   456	        }
   457	    }
   458	
   459	    private BufferData readNextChunk(HttpPrologue prologue, WritableHeaders<?> headers) {
   460	        // chunk length processing
   461	        String hex = reader.readLine();
   462	        int chunkLength = ParserHelper.parseNonNegative(hex, 16, INVALID_SIZE_EXCEPTION_SUPPLIER);
   463	
   464	        currentEntitySizeRead += chunkLength;
   465	        if (maxPayloadSize != -1 && currentEntitySizeRead > maxPayloadSize) {
   466	            throw RequestException.builder()
   467	                    .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   468	                    .status(Status.REQUEST_ENTITY_TOO_LARGE_413)
   469	                    .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   470	                    .setKeepAlive(false)
   471	                    .build();
   472	        }
   473	        // read chunk
   474	        if (chunkLength == 0) {
   475	            String end = reader.readLine();
   476	            if (!end.isEmpty()) {
   477	                throw RequestException.builder()
   478	                        .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   479	                        .message("Invalid terminating chunk")
   480	                        .build();
   481	            }
   482	            return null;
   483	        }
   484	        BufferData nextChunkData = reader.readBuffer(chunkLength);
   485	        reader.skip(2); // skip \r\n after the chunk
   486	        return nextChunkData;
   487	    }
   488	
   489	    private BufferData readLengthEntity() {
   490	        long stillNeed = currentEntitySize - currentEntitySizeRead;
   491	        if (stillNeed == 0) {
   492	            return null;
   493	        }
   494	
   495	        reader.ensureAvailable();
   496	        int toRead = (int) Math.min(reader.available(), stillNeed);
   497	        BufferData buffer = reader.readBuffer(toRead);
   498	        this.currentEntitySizeRead += toRead;
   499	        return buffer;
   500	    }
   501	
   502	    private void route(HttpPrologue prologue,
   503	                       WritableHeaders<?> headers,
   504	                       LimitAlgorithm.Outcome limitOutcome) {
   505	        EntityStyle entity = EntityStyle.NONE;
   506	
   507	        if (headers.contains(HeaderValues.TRANSFER_ENCODING_CHUNKED)) {
   508	            entity = EntityStyle.CHUNKED;
   509	            this.currentEntitySize = -1;
   510	        } else if (headers.contains(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH)) {
   511	            try {
   512	                this.currentEntitySize = headers.get(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH).get(long.class);
   513	                if (maxPayloadSize != -1 && currentEntitySize > maxPayloadSize) {
   514	                    throw RequestException.builder()
   515	                            .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   516	                            .status(Status.REQUEST_ENTITY_TOO_LARGE_413)
   517	                            .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   518	                            .setKeepAlive(false)
   519	                            .build();
   520	                }
   521	                entity = currentEntitySize == 0 ? EntityStyle.NONE : EntityStyle.LENGTH;
   522	            } catch (MapperException e) {
   523	                throw RequestException.builder()
   524	                        .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   525	                        .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   526	                        .message("Content length is not a number")
   527	                        .cause(e)
   528	                        .build();
   529	            }
   530	        }
   531	        requestId++;
   532	
   533	        if (entity == EntityStyle.NONE) {
   534	            Http1ServerRequest request = Http1ServerRequest.create(ctx,
   535	                                                                   routing.security(),
   536	                                                                   prologue,
   537	                                                                   headers,
   538	                                                                   requestId,
   539	                                                                   limitOutcome);
   540	
   541	            Http1ServerResponse response = new Http1ServerResponse(ctx,
   542	                                                                   sendListener,
   543	                                                                   writer,
   544	                                                                   request,
   545	                                                                   !headers.contains(HeaderValues.CONNECTION_CLOSE),
   546	                                                                   http1Config.validateResponseHeaders());
   547	
   548	            routing.route(ctx, request, response);
   549	            // we have handled a request without request entity
   550	            return;
   551	        }
   552	
   553	        boolean expectContinue = false;
   554	
   555	        // Expect: 100-continue
   556	        if (headers.contains(HeaderValues.EXPECT_100)) {
   557	            if (this.http1Config.continueImmediately()) {
   558	                try {
   559	                    writer.writeNow(BufferData.create(CONTINUE_100));
   560	                } catch (UncheckedIOException e) {
   561	                    throw new ServerConnectionException("Failed to write continue", e);
   562	                }
   563	            }
   564	            expectContinue = true;
   565	        }
   566	
   567	        ContentDecoder decoder;
   568	        if (contentEncodingContext.contentDecodingEnabled()) {
   569	            // there may be some decoder used
   570	            if (headers.contains(HeaderNames.CONTENT_ENCODING)) {
   571	                String contentEncoding = headers.get(HeaderNames.CONTENT_ENCODING).get();
   572	                if (contentEncodingContext.contentDecodingSupported(contentEncoding)) {
   573	                    decoder = contentEncodingContext.decoder(contentEncoding);
   574	                } else {
   575	                    throw RequestException.builder()
   576	                            .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   577	                            .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   578	                            .message("Unsupported content encoding")
   579	                            .build();
   580	                }
   581	            } else {
   582	                decoder = ContentDecoder.NO_OP;
   583	            }
   584	        } else {
   585	            // Check whether Content-Encoding header is present when headers validation is enabled
   586	            if (http1Config.validateRequestHeaders() && headers.contains(HeaderNames.CONTENT_ENCODING)) {
   587	                throw RequestException.builder()
   588	                        .type(EventType.BAD_REQUEST)
   589	                        .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   590	                        .message("Content-Encoding header present when content encoding is disabled")
   591	                        .build();
   592	            }
   593	            decoder = ContentDecoder.NO_OP;
   594	        }
   595	
   596	        CountDownLatch entityReadLatch = new CountDownLatch(1);
   597	        Http1ServerRequest request = Http1ServerRequest.create(ctx,
   598	                                                               this,
   599	                                                               http1Config,
   600	                                                               routing.security(),
   601	                                                               prologue,
   602	                                                               ServerRequestHeaders.create(headers),
   603	                                                               decoder,
   604	                                                               requestId,
   605	                                                               expectContinue,
   606	                                                               entityReadLatch,
   607	                                                               () -> this.readEntityFromPipeline(prologue, headers),
   608	                                                               limitOutcome);
   609	        Http1ServerResponse response = new Http1ServerResponse(ctx,
   610	                                                               sendListener,
   611	                                                               writer,
   612	                                                               request,
   613	                                                               !request.headers()
   614	                                                                       .contains(HeaderValues.CONNECTION_CLOSE),
   615	                                                               http1Config.validateResponseHeaders());
   616	
   617	        routing.route(ctx, request, response);
   618	
   619	        consumeEntity(request, response, entityReadLatch);
   620	        try {
   621	            entityReadLatch.await();
   622	        } catch (InterruptedException e) {
   623	            throw RequestException.builder()
   624	                    .type(EventType.INTERNAL_ERROR)
   625	                    .request(DirectTransportRequest.create(prologue, headers))
   626	                    .message("Failed to wait for pipeline")
   627	                    .cause(e)
   628	                    .build();
   629	        }
   630	    }
   631	
   632	    private void consumeEntity(Http1ServerRequest request, Http1ServerResponse response, CountDownLatch entityReadLatch) {
   633	        if (response.headers().contains(HeaderValues.CONNECTION_CLOSE) || request.content().consumed()) {
   634	            // we do not care about request entity if connection is getting closed
   635	            entityReadLatch.countDown();
   636	            return;
   637	        }
   638	        // consume the entity if not consumed by routing
   639	        try {
   640	            request.content().consume();
   641	        } catch (Exception e) {
   642	            boolean keepAlive = request.content().consumed() && response.headers().contains(HeaderValues.CONNECTION_KEEP_ALIVE);
   643	            // we must close connection, as we could not consume request
   644	            if (!response.isSent()) {
   645	                throw new InternalServerException(e.getMessage(), e, keepAlive);
   646	            }
   647	            throw new CloseConnectionException("Failed to consume request entity, must close", e);
   648	        }
   649	    }
   650	
   651	    private void handleRequestException(RequestException e) {
   652	        // gather error handling properties
   653	        ErrorHandling errorHandling = ctx.listenerContext()
   654	                .config()
   655	                .errorHandling();
   656	
   657	        // log message in DEBUG mode
   658	        if (LOGGER.isLoggable(DEBUG) && (e.safeMessage() || errorHandling.logAllMessages())) {
   659	            LOGGER.log(DEBUG, e);
   660	        }
   661	
   662	        // create message to return based on settings
   663	        String message = null;
   664	        if (errorHandling.includeEntity()) {
   665	            message = e.safeMessage() ? e.getMessage() : "Bad request, see server log for more information";
   666	        }
   667	
   668	        // handle exception condition using direct handlers
   669	        DirectHandler handler = ctx.listenerContext()
   670	                .directHandlers()
   671	                .handler(e.eventType());
   672	        DirectHandler.TransportResponse response = handler.handle(e.request(),
   673	                                                                  e.eventType(),
   674	                                                                  e.status(),
   675	                                                                  e.responseHeaders(),
   676	                                                                  message);
   677	
   678	        // write response
   679	        BufferData buffer = BufferData.growing(128);
   680	        ServerResponseHeaders headers = response.headers();
   681	
   682	        // we are escaping the connection loop, the connection will be closed
   683	        headers.set(HeaderValues.CONNECTION_CLOSE);
   684	
   685	        byte[] entity = response.entity().orElse(BufferData.EMPTY_BYTES);
   686	        headers.set(HeaderValues.create(HeaderNames.CONTENT_LENGTH, String.valueOf(entity.length)));
   687	
   688	        Http1ServerResponse.nonEntityBytes(headers, response.status(), buffer, response.keepAlive(),
   689	                                           http1Config.validateResponseHeaders());
   690	        if (entity.length != 0) {
   691	            buffer.write(entity);
   692	        }
   693	
   694	        sendListener.status(ctx, response.status());
   695	        sendListener.headers(ctx, headers);
   696	        sendListener.data(ctx, buffer);
   697	        try {
   698	            writer.write(buffer);
   699	        } catch (UncheckedIOException uioe) {
   700	            throw new ServerConnectionException("Failed to write request exception", uioe);
   701	        }
   702	
   703	        if (response.status() == Status.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR_500) {
   704	            LOGGER.log(WARNING, "Internal server error", e);
   705	        }
   706	    }
   707	}

    53	import io.helidon.webserver.spi.ServerConnection;
